  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_e9f74593-0e4e-4439-9e59-781acbc7706d'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer4880999923618071491">Ryan Kendall is broken. He understands pain. He knows the hand of violence and the ache of loss. He knows what it means to fail those who need you. Being broken doesn’t stop him wanting the one thing he can’t have; Finlay Tanner. Her smile is sweet and her future bright. She’s the girl he grew up with, the girl he loves, the girl he protects from the world, and from himsel</span>
  <span id="freeText4880999923618071491" style="display:none">Ryan Kendall is broken. He understands pain. He knows the hand of violence and the ache of loss. He knows what it means to fail those who need you. Being broken doesn’t stop him wanting the one thing he can’t have; Finlay Tanner. Her smile is sweet and her future bright. She’s the girl he grew up with, the girl he loves, the girl he protects from the world, and from himself.<br /><br />At nineteen, Ryan leaves to join the Australian Army. After years of training he becomes an elite SAS soldier and deploys to the Afghanistan war. His patrol undertakes the most dangerous missions a soldier can face. But no matter how far he runs, or how hard he fights, his need for Finlay won’t let go.<br /><br />Returning home after six years, one look is all it takes to know he can’t live without her. But sometimes love isn’t enough to heal what hurts. Sometimes people like him can’t be fixed, and sometimes people like Finlay deserve more than what’s left.<br /><br />This is a story about war and the cost of sacrifice. Where bonds are formed, and friendships found. Where those who are strong, fall hard. Where love is let go, heartache is born, and heroes are made. Where one man learns that the hardest fight of all, is the fight to save himself.</span>

This is all in all a romance novel. Do read it, you won't regret it. It's just a beautiful story worth reading<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

Powerful, captivating and emotionally charged, this book is a must-read!! </b><br/><br/>It's an unforgettable story about a broken soldier's undying love for a woman who'd always held his heart and it is truly breathtaking!<br/><br/>I just want to shout from the rooftops -- READ THIS BOOK, EVERYONE!!!!<br/><br/>You will FEEL this story it with your whole heart.<br/><br/>I can almost guarantee that</span>
  <span id="freeText9396884172373370265" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386181636i/7308148._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> 5++ STARS!!!! THIS IS A MUST READ!!! </b><br><br>First, here are some casting pics...<br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386064524ra/7283915.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386064728i/7283942.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386064524i/7283917._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><i>Fighting Redemption</i> was everything I could want in a story and more!! Powerful, captivating and emotionally charged, this book is a must-read!! </b><br><br>It's an unforgettable story about a broken soldier's undying love for a woman who'd always held his heart and it is truly breathtaking!<br><br>I just want to shout from the rooftops -- READ THIS BOOK, EVERYONE!!!!<br><br>You will FEEL this story it with your whole heart.<br><br>I can almost guarantee that you'll cry while reading (probably several times) because the story is truly heart wrenching but I promise you that it's worth every tear and that you'll be left with a smile on your face.<br><br>My eyes were already filled with tears from the very first pages. The prologue alone was all it took for me to fully <em>connect</em> and I knew right from the start that this book was going to be special.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Even though we've never been together, you've always been mine, and even if I never get to keep you, you'll still be mine."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Ryan had dreamed his whole life of becoming a soldier. With a drunken father who beat him and fought constantly with his mother, he couldn't wait to get away. Then Finlay walked into his life -- and she was this gorgeous, shining beacon that called to his heart. But as much as he was in love with her, he couldn't allow himself to have her because his whole life had been building towards the dream of getting out and away; of becoming a solider. And at 19, he left everything behind and joined the Army.<br><br>Six years went by as he trained, fought, saved lives, took lives, survived, and lived through hell but he never stopped thinking about the girl he'd aways wanted, who'd never been his but who owned his heart... and that he'd walked away from.<br><br>And then... he came home.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>
      <strong>"For six years I fought every day not to think of you, and I lost, because every day you were all I could see."</strong>
    </em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Honestly, I'm being <em>very</em> vague about the storyline here because there is <em>so</em> much more to it that I really think will be better enjoyed if you just discover it for yourself along the way.<br><br>The story unfolded beautifully. It was captivating. It began by giving us a heart-wrenching taste of the future, and then took us right back to the very beginning showing how the relationships intensified over the years and allowing us to fall in love with them as they were falling in love with each other.<br><br>It was gorgeous but made my heart ache watching Ryan's quiet, unspoken love for Fin grow throughout his childhood. I <em>felt</em> his longing so strongly and these built-up feelings were a huge part of what made everything <em>so</em> powerful once their love for each other was acknowledged.<br><br>I can't even tell you how many different things I felt while I was reading this. The writing was effortless and enthralling and I felt like I was watching a movie of the events rather than just reading them. Every scene came alive in my mind as though it were happening right in front of me.<br><br><em>Everything</em>  in this story was just so emotionally charged. I felt every word of this book. My heart fluttered, raced, pounded, and even stopped. It was beaten, bruised, broken and then put back together.<br><br>It was just beat after beat of these hugely <em>powerful</em> moments and I'd stop every few pages to just let them all sink in. Sometimes I'd even go back and immediately reread a section because it had hit me so strongly that I just wanted to keep reliving it.<br><br>Ryan and Fin were true soul mates. I'm crying even as I write this because what they had - their <i>connection </i> - was just so. fucking. powerful. So often, I'd be reading a scene that wasn't even sad but suddenly tears would be pouring down my face just from emotional overflow.<br><br>Here are just some snippets...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I miss you. Each day hurts a little more than the last."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>And this...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Fin. Look at me," Ryan said firmly.</em>
    <br>
    <em>She lifted her eyes.</em>
    <br>
    <em>"Just one day at a time, okay?"</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>And ohh my gosh -- <em>this:</em><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I'll love you longer than the stars that live in the sky."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>There was also one scene in particular that made me ugly cry. And by that I mean that I had to put my book down because I literally could not see the page through my tears. I was a shaking, sobbing wreck. But I loved every minute. Books that can pull <em>this</em> level of emotional out of me are the ones that stay in my heart.<br><br>The story took place over many years and was always moving forward but, at the same time, it always slowed down and took the time to highlight all the important, meaningful parts of their lives.<br><br>There were so many gorgeous visual moment that just stood out to me: the Black Hawk helicopter -- Ryan holding his hand out to Fin -- Fin cleaning his wounds in her bedroom -- that moment when Jake asked Ryan if he was in love with Fin -- the dance -- <em>that</em> night -- lying under the stars -- the letter -- <em>ALL THE LETTERS!!!!!</em> -- the lawn scene -- Brothers forever -- the tarmac -- .... pieces of this beautiful story just keeps playing over and over in my head and honestly, I don't want them to stop.<br><br>Sacrifice, loyalty, strength, redemption, loss, <em>
  <strong>love </strong>
</em>... This book had it all and more.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Every piece of me is in here... My breath, my heart, my life. I won't ever leave you if you keep that safe inside you."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>When I finished, I just sat there letting the story sink in, letting the tears pour down my face, <em>feeling</em> the journey -- the heart ache, the loss, the happiness....<br><br><em>This</em> is the kind of book that I spend all my time searching for. Reading this beautifully written and absolutely unforgettable story is an experience that will stay with me forever.<br><br>I <i>highly</i> recommend it!! In fact, I'll just say -- READ IT!!!!! You <em>all</em> should read this!! ♥<br><br><strong>Rating: 5++ stars</strong><br><br>** This is a standalone (Adult) romance with a HEA.<br><br>****************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="9396884172373370265" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1110269656" />
    <a title="Jessica&#39;s Totally Over The Top Book Obsession" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28967089-jessica-s-totally-over-the-top-book-obsession"><img alt="Jessica&#39;s Totally Over The Top Book Obsession" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1511556834p2/28967089.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1110269656?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica&#39;s Totally Over The Top Book Obsession" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica&#39;s Totally Over The Top Book Obsession" href="/user/show/28967089-jessica-s-totally-over-the-top-book-obsession">Jessica&#39;s Totally Over The Top Book Obsession</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28967089-jessica-s-totally-over-the-top-book-obsession?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28967089-jessica-s-totally-over-the-top-book-obsession?shelf=meh-reads">meh-reads</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1110269656" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer502908646857595761"><b>2.5 Just didn't work for me Stars</b><br/><br/><b> * Spoilers below* </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/861502_zps54uqiji3.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444571675ra/16519108.gif' alt=' photo 861502_zps54uqiji3.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I feel like the odd man out here. Like everyone of my Goodreads Friends loved this book. Like they wanted to give it 6 stars out of 5. I wanted to like this book so much. I mean it has some of my favorite things in it. Military men, a baby, love each other their whole life and best friend's sister. I mean it had all the makings for me to think I would love it, but I didn't. I was about 10% into the book when I knew my ass was in trouble, bu</span>
  <span id="freeText502908646857595761" style="display:none"><b>2.5 Just didn't work for me Stars</b><br><br><b> * Spoilers below* </b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/861502_zps54uqiji3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444571675ra/16519108.gif" alt=" photo 861502_zps54uqiji3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I feel like the odd man out here. Like everyone of my Goodreads Friends loved this book. Like they wanted to give it 6 stars out of 5. I wanted to like this book so much. I mean it has some of my favorite things in it. Military men, a baby, love each other their whole life and best friend's sister. I mean it had all the makings for me to think I would love it, but I didn't. I was about 10% into the book when I knew my ass was in trouble, but I held out because I hoped the love would redeem all the other stuff that bugged me. It didn't. This book hit on so many of my pet peeves, cheating, cowardly fear making one of the MC push the other away to an extreme, and long separation of the H&amp;H. Add in all the drama, and angst, and not nearly enough happy moments to balance it out. This book just left me sad, annoyed, and unsatisfied.<br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/7345540_zpspb54n8cf.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444571675ra/16519109.gif" alt=" photo 7345540_zpspb54n8cf.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Before I start to tell you what all didn't work for me in this book let me just say that even though this book wasn't my jam, I could tell by the writing that the author is extremely talented and that I would try other books by her. That being said here is a list of all the things in this book that left a bitter taste in my mouth and ruined this read for me.<br><br>1. Fin loses her virginity to her bf Ian who is not the hero Ryan. It is written in great detail her making love to Ian, not Ryan. And even though they are not together, they both already have feelings for each other. Also it may not have bugged me so much if her being with another man wasn't so detailed. <br><br>2. Ryan leaves for 6 years without saying a word to her. For 6 years no letters, no email, no calls nothing. <br><br>3. I feel so bad for Ian. Fin does him dirty. Fin dates Ian for years, but when he wants to move in together and take the next step because he is madly in love with her she holds him at arms length. Then when Ryan comes home after 6 years of cutting her off, she lets Ryan touch her and kiss her. Yes she does stop before sleeping with him , but if you have a bf and you're kissing someone else and they have their hand on your breast,and ass, and you are kissing them back it's cheating. It felt like she used Ian as a filler, because she couldn't have who she really wanted. <br><br>4. Ryan drove me crazy the way he wanted Fin but would push her away, want her, nope not good enough for her, but I want, can't have her, I can't live without her, I will leave for her own good ......blah blah blah. I felt like the book went in circles. Ryan acting like a coward causes Fin and himself a ton of pain, and made me wanna slam my head into a wall.<br><br>5. Ryan doesn't man the fuck up until almost the end of the book and only after he finds out she is pregnant. <br><br>6. The story jumps around a lot. 5 years here, 6 months there, 2 months here, 8 weeks there, on and on. I felt like I was missing big chucks of the story. I can understand jumping forward every once in a while in a story, there are so many in this book it's crazy.<br><br><br>All that being said there was some moments in this book that totally broke my heart and had me emotional, and there was some sweet moments with Fin and Ryan, I loved Jake, and the writing was good. And for those reasons I am giving this book a 2.5 stars. Though I didn't really get into this book I didn't hate it. I just dislike more about it than I liked. I am the minority in my views on this book and almost all my friends loved it so I would tell anyone who wants to read it to go for it. <br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://jessicasoverthetopbookobsession.blogspot.com/2016/02/fighting-redemption.html">http://jessicasoverthetopbookobsessio...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="502908646857595761" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer751321743" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer12241166419197253726"> <b>5 STARS</b><br/><br/>I re-read fighting redemption and I can honestly say that I LOVED every minute of it!!! Fighting Redemption is a story of family, friendship, love, loss and pain.The story will take you on a wild ride, you'll be happy one minute and then crying in the next , and then again you are happy!!<br/>I really love stories like this because the emotions you feel are so real. All the characters are so genuine, that you want the best for them! After having read this book I finally understand how difficu</span>
  <span id="freeText12241166419197253726" style="display:none"> <b>5 STARS</b><br><br>I re-read fighting redemption and I can honestly say that I LOVED every minute of it!!! Fighting Redemption is a story of family, friendship, love, loss and pain.The story will take you on a wild ride, you'll be happy one minute and then crying in the next , and then again you are happy!!<br>I really love stories like this because the emotions you feel are so real. All the characters are so genuine, that you want the best for them! After having read this book I finally understand how difficult is, having a loved one who is in the military because everyday you're afraid because you might never see them again. They might die at war and you might never get the chance to say goodbye...<br><br><b>"I'll love you longer than the stars that live in the sky."</b><br><br><br>The story is about three friends.. Ryan, Jake and his sister Finlay.Finlay and her older brother Jake meet Ryan Kendall on their new school. Jake and Ryan become instant best friends.Finlay and Ryan, both have feelings for each other..<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384518834i/6892916.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ryan and Jake decide to join the army.For Finlay, it wasn't enough heartache that her brother and his best friend were going off to Afghanistan,also she had to deal with her feelings for Ryan..<br>I loved the relationship that the three of them had. The bond and love is so unconditional.<br>Ryan and Finlay's story broke my heart over and over :(((<br>Finlay is torn by wanting and loving Ryan or moving on... <br><br><b>"For six years I fought every day not to think of you, and I lost, because every day you were all I could see."<br><br>“When I’m near you I’m consumed by you—your smile, your eyes, your heart. Even though we’ve never been together, you’ve always been mine, and ever if I never get to keep you, you’ll still be mine.”</b><br><br>After a tragedy... :( Ryan and Finlay admit their feelings to each other and they became a couple...but this it wasn't easy..They are two so opposite characters,yet so perfect match at the same time. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386263729ra/7325001.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ryan omg :// I love him!!!He lived with such an awful pain inside of him!He was physically and mentally abused by his father. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386263729ra/7325002.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ryan's only dream was to become soldier...but then he finds his family with the Tanners and love with Finlay.Finlay is a new light in his soul and heart...Finlay and Ryan wouldn't be together without Jake...I liked him so much.He was so open and he was all for Ryan and Fin because he wanted them to be together and happy...<br><br>If you are looking for a beautiful,emotionally romance this is what you need!!This is a MUST READ!!! </span>

<div id="review_720900513" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/720900513" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/720900513?book_show_action=true">Sep 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=new-adult-express">new-adult-express</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=contemporary-duckie">contemporary-duckie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=i-trust-my-friends">i-trust-my-friends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=die-from-angst">die-from-angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=oops-let-s-do-it-again-romance">oops-let-s-do-it-again-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=military-romance">military-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=third-time-s-the-charm-romance">third-time-s-the-charm-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer720900513" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18280371422352438218"><b>2.5-3 stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405334774i/10383254._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>About 7 months ago, I received a Christmas present: an ebook of <u>Fighting Redemption</u> emailed to me from my mom who read and loved it after seeing it on Amazon’s recommendation list. Our tastes almost never converge so seeing her love a military romance <i>really</i> brought this book to my attention. It was also impossible to ignore all the reviews and status updates about the book – almost everyone who did read it ugly cried and said it was a top favorite of the year. I told myself right th</span>
  <span id="freeText18280371422352438218" style="display:none"><b>2.5-3 stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405334774i/10383254._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>About 7 months ago, I received a Christmas present: an ebook of <u>Fighting Redemption</u> emailed to me from my mom who read and loved it after seeing it on Amazon’s recommendation list. Our tastes almost never converge so seeing her love a military romance <i>really</i> brought this book to my attention. It was also impossible to ignore all the reviews and status updates about the book – almost everyone who did read it ugly cried and said it was a top favorite of the year. I told myself right then and there that I would wait at least half a year to read it: I didn’t want the hype and the bandwagon effect to cloud my reading experience. So yeah, this book scared the crap out of me. But there was never a doubt in my mind that YES, this is the kind of story that I wanted to read. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405334585i/10383242._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So now that I’ve finished the book, I’m mulling it over in my head. It took me almost 3 days to read and I’ve DNFed twice before picking it up again. Also cried twice. The very first thing I noted was that Kate McCarthy is an extremely talented writer. I’ll admit she is very brilliant with her words so it’s easy to get lost in the wave of emotions her writing evokes, especially when it came to the numerous obstacles keeping Fin and Ryan from each other. Except…now that I think about it, <i>I never understood their love for each other in the first place.</i> For me, they go from children growing up together, having the occasional conversation/interaction, hit puberty and had crushes on each other (NEITHER voiced their feelings), then Ryan went off to war and Fin got herself a boyfriend. Now 6 years later, they see each other and immediately start professing ‘I’ll-die-for-you’ love?  Where’d that come from?? So right off the bat, that was a big disconnect for me.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405334585i/10383243._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It doesn’t matter that Fin knew she had feelings for Ryan, Ryan knew he had feelings for Fin, and I knew they both had feelings for each other. They never gave weight to that “love,” never voiced it until it was too late. Another thing was the third person POV. I’m usually not too picky about the POVs but for some reason, third person here only served to sever any possible connection I had with these characters so for the entire book I never was invested in their story. That beginning made their love seem a bit insta-ish and then the writing style just wasn’t my thing. I also despise time gaps and lemme tell you, there are tons in here. The one that absolutely pissed me off and marked my first DNF was <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[when the author fast-forwarded the story to ‘6 months later’ after Fin comes back from her trip from Antarctica and immediately breaks up with her boyfriend Ian. I literally just read about Ian and Fin in the last chapter.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Do authors slap a ‘_____ months later’ at the beginning of a chapter and seriously expect readers to assume there was plot &amp; character development in between? To me, time gaps and this one in particular is a sign of lazy storytelling. <br><br>But like I said, I cried twice. Too bad both times I cried they were for dead characters, not the couple in question. However, my heartstrings were tugged at in certain scenes like the parts where Ryan was off at war or the very rare parts where raw, heartfelt emotion was displayed.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405334585i/10383244._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It always disappoints me when I don’t love a book as much as my friends do. No one wants to feel like a lone wolf but honestly, I just did not click with this book. Perhaps if I read it all those months ago my outlook would be different. But since I read it now, all I can say is unfortunately, this book didn’t wow me and isn’t anything I haven’t read before. <br><br>P.S. My second DNF mark was when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Fin got pregnant (because that’s what happens when you don’t use a condom) and wasn’t able to tell Ryan because he was being a noble asshole running off again. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>P.P.S. Not sure why I felt like adding this but I guess it’s just one of those trust-your-gut ideas. Anyways, this review is in no way trying to diminish or trivialize the sacrifices, experiences, and efforts soldiers make for their country. Its sole purpose is to express my somewhat dissatisfied reading experience regarding this particular book.<br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="18280371422352438218" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_718823989" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/718823989" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/718823989?book_show_action=true">Sep 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=cover-lust-i-has-it">cover-lust-i-has-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=review-copy">review-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=tortured-abused-hero">tortured-abused-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=shower-smexin">shower-smexin</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=military-romance">military-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer718823989" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16448160190936691588"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384327404i/6849860._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo FightingRedemptionTeaser4_zps05ac4261.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>It’s nigh on impossible to put into words how much I loved this book and how much it touched me. It’s a compelling story of love and loss, incredible happiness and crippling sadness, a gut-wrenching, tear-jerking emotional roller-coaster of a ride which I was unable to put down once I’d started and I read into the wee small hours of the morning to finish this because I just had to know how it ended. Better perhaps to say that I dreaded how it was gong to end. In fact I feared the ending, right </span>
  <span id="freeText16448160190936691588" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384327404i/6849860._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo FightingRedemptionTeaser4_zps05ac4261.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>It’s nigh on impossible to put into words how much I loved this book and how much it touched me. It’s a compelling story of love and loss, incredible happiness and crippling sadness, a gut-wrenching, tear-jerking emotional roller-coaster of a ride which I was unable to put down once I’d started and I read into the wee small hours of the morning to finish this because I just had to know how it ended. Better perhaps to say that I dreaded how it was gong to end. In fact I feared the ending, right after reading the prologue which, I have to confess, had me crying by page two! I felt instinctively that I was about to embark on something really special and Fighting Redemption absolutely delivered.<br><br>I am a big fan of Kate McCarthy’s – I’ve loved and adored her books before. You know you’re going to get fantastic characters – heroes and heroines that seem real and a captivating plot but I think it’s fair to say that she outdid herself with Fighting Redemption. I had high expectations going in and I wasn’t disappointed but she’s definitely raised the bar exponentially higher now than ever before but I have confidence in her ability to deliver. Fighting Redemption is unforgettable, powerful, incredibly moving and it will live on my heart for months and years to come.<br><br>So this is Ryan and Finlay’s story – thrown together by chance and circumstances in childhood, they have practically grown up together. Ever since that first day when Fin stumbled at school in front of him, she has triggered every protective instinct in Ryan and he has loved her and only her for as long as he can remember. Ryan has endured a painful childhood that really did make my heart hurt but he has an incredible friendship with Fin’s older brother Jake that finally offers him salvation from his situation as he practically grows up with them.<br><br>As grown men Ryan and Jake join the Army, rise to the ranks of the S.A.S and go off to fight in Afghanistan. The horrors of war, the deep effects on those who serve and those left behind are powerfully served up here – it’s gritty, realistic and harsh and you had better get the Kleenex on standby. I cried buckets!<br><br>I adored Ryan – his incredible strength both physical and emotional, his restraint, his awesome physique and just the way that he loved, adored and cherished Fin. It really was a thing of beauty. He’s constantly trying to do what he thinks is the right thing by Fin, often being selfless and sacrificing his own happiness for what he thinks is best for her. He’s a soulful, passionate and very sexy hero and, for the longest time, the simmering sexual tension between the two of them is almost palpable – it’s unacted upon for years although they are deeply longing for one another but constantly denied but, when they finally can resist it no longer, their connection is incendiary and white-hot!!<br><br>Fin is a heroine after my own heart. I identified with her closely. She’s a clumsy nerd just like me – in fact, this is pretty much my favourite combination in a book - the geeky heroine and the tough alpha hero. Fin is a sweetheart – unfailingly honest and incredibly generous and giving. It’s no wonder Ryan adores her. She has much to endure in this book and so much to lose. My heart hurt for her on so many occasions and, as I neared the end, I was so afraid of how things would turn out.<br><br>I’m a military wife myself and Kate McCarthy really does a fantastic job of showing just how hard it is for the family left behind as the soldiers go off to war. The fear, the pride and the long months spent apart are vividly recreated here – it’s incredibly realistic and spoke to me on a very personal level. The whole story did – it touched my heart in a way that very few books have ever managed to before and I am never going to forget this one.<br><br>As with any Kate McCarthy book, this story was hard to put down. She writes incredibly compelling and captivating plots and her writing style and the pacing are perfect and I just allowed this story to roll over me, never once really knowing how it was going to end but preparing myself for the worst. It’s been one of the highlights of my reading year and one of the best books I’ve ever read. It’s just exquisite.<br><br>5 stars – 6 if I could!<p>
  <em>
    <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/2013/12/guest-post-release-day-review.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">See this review at Sinfully Sexy</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer779928868" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17527650762225087398"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386211241i/7313136._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>I'll love you longer than the stars that live in the sky </b> <br/><br/><br/>What a beautiful unforgettable story ❤️<br/><br/><br/>This is a story about war and the cost of sacrifice. Where bonds are formed, and friendships found. Where those who are strong, fall hard. Where love is let go, heartache is born, and heroes are made. Where one man learns that the hardest fight of all, is the fight to save himself.<br/><br/><br/>Ohhh<br/>My<br/>God<br/><br/>Goodbye heart ❤️<br/><br/>He couldn’t think of Fin as his. He couldn’t feel that way. Ryan had to focus on fighting his wa</span>
  <span id="freeText17527650762225087398" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386211241i/7313136._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I'll love you longer than the stars that live in the sky </b> <br><br><br>What a beautiful unforgettable story ❤️<br><br><br>This is a story about war and the cost of sacrifice. Where bonds are formed, and friendships found. Where those who are strong, fall hard. Where love is let go, heartache is born, and heroes are made. Where one man learns that the hardest fight of all, is the fight to save himself.<br><br><br>Ohhh<br>My<br>God<br><br>Goodbye heart ❤️<br><br>He couldn’t think of Fin as his. He couldn’t feel that way. Ryan had to focus on fighting his way out of this town. How could he do that if Fin owned his heart? <br><br>Fin ~ beautiful clumsy nerd ..... She loved Ryan her whole life. There was so much genuine adoration between these two that I could not stop sighhhhing and then crying and then full-out wailing. I love this book with all my heart. This is my signature read. Weepy-steamy ...... Holy F ! This book wrecked me. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br><blockquote> <br>“I’d give almost anything to wake up to that every morning.”<br>He hated the words that came out of his mouth. It hurt like a bitch knowing her beautiful smile belonged to another man.<br>“Almost anything.” She backed up a step. “That’s always been our problem, hasn’t it?”<br> <br><br><br><b> “When I’m near you I’m consumed by you—your smile, your eyes, your heart. Even though we’ve never been together, you’ve always been mine, and even if I never get to keep you, you’ll still be mine. " </b> <br><br><br>“Enough!” She jabbed a finger in his chest. “There’s hurt in there. I know it. You know it, but you’re not going to move on from it until you let that shit out. Whatever you’re doing now isn’t working. Own it, Ryan. Stop letting it own you.”</blockquote><br><br>This book is too beautiful to review without being very vague and giving away too much! I'm still crying ! I can't stop thinking about this book !!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386214654i/7313706.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386214958i/7313748._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="17527650762225087398" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer11152852720824241513"> <b>WARNING SPOILERS<br/><br/>READER BE AWARE THESE ARE ONLY MY PERSONAL FEELINGS THAT WERE SO PAINFULLY BRUISED, BUT MAY NOT BE BRUISED FOR YOU WHEN YOU WILL READ THIS BOOK!</b><br/><br/><br/><b>I am so devastated!!!!!!!</b><br/><br/>I am so utterly angry and frustrated...it hurts me more with each page.....I wish i new that before reading this book...<br/><br/>I cannot stand the fact....that we need to read about both Hero and heroine sleeping with someone else..whilst secretly loved each other..its just so unromantic and unappealing...Ok he loves her</span>
  <span id="freeText11152852720824241513" style="display:none"> <b>WARNING SPOILERS<br /><br />READER BE AWARE THESE ARE ONLY MY PERSONAL FEELINGS THAT WERE SO PAINFULLY BRUISED, BUT MAY NOT BE BRUISED FOR YOU WHEN YOU WILL READ THIS BOOK!</b><br /><br /><br /><b>I am so devastated!!!!!!!</b><br /><br />I am so utterly angry and frustrated...it hurts me more with each page.....I wish i new that before reading this book...<br /><br />I cannot stand the fact....that we need to read about both Hero and heroine sleeping with someone else..whilst secretly loved each other..its just so unromantic and unappealing...Ok he loves her..but still he does not mind having sex with other girls? YEAH RIGHT....But NO it does not work for me like that... and on top of that..we are forced to read explicit details of heroine giving her virginity to someone else she does not love.. I should not be subjected to that...because that's not what i am expecting from my romance...those sex scenes should not be there in such a details...it really breaks my heart...because it felt wrong that its not the "hero" but some other guy... Then to add more punches....when the hero is back from the war again we have to read about her being with her boyfriend and of course having sex...but to be with her boyfriend the entire book??? Where is the romance between her and the "Hero"? <b>WHAT A TURN OFF!...</b> I hate love triangle because I know "each characters" will suffer from it and one will suffer the most .....I don't want to read about both characters sleeping with someone else and having that image in my head!!!!!!!!! NO NO NO All I want is to read about <b>"THEM" hero and heroine making love and NOT WITH SOMEONE ELSE.......</b> Its true that some of these traits add hints of realism to the novel, but this book is a romance novel, hence its design is to inspire fantasy and a feeling of enjoyment, I felt none of this...and quite frankly I felt more interested and invested with the "hero" fighting in the army...it provided me with some relief from the explicit sex scenes with heroine and OM...but that is not what i should be doing...I should not feel like "avoiding my characters"...I want to feel joy and excitement when engaging with my protagonists..but that's not what happened here! <br /><br />I had so much hopes for this book and I cannot denied it puled me emotionally...but its not enough for me to feel <b>"enjoyment"</b> when i should feel the need to be with my "characters" every step of the way...and I cannot feel that here..because I want to escape from the real world and feel something that will make me forget about harsh reality and this book wants me to escape to reality! </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer824362797" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13656499037808577300"><br/><br/><b>6 Outstanding, blow my mind stars ******</b><br/> <br/><b>
  <blockquote> Family, friendship, love, loyalty, protect, strength, PAIN</blockquote>
</b><br/> <br/><a href='http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/fighting%20redemption/lovewords_zps5146576e.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390079751i/8140223._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo lovewords_zps5146576e.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/> <br/><b>
  <i>This is a well thought out, well put together story that gives you glimpses into the effect of being a soldier, what its like to be a family who has members that are in the SAS plus what a military wife/lover goes through when your heart is literally put on the line every time your love could be taken right away from you at any moment. <br/>This story ripped open my heart, I cried full pel</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText13656499037808577300" style="display:none"><br><br><b>6 Outstanding, blow my mind stars ******</b><br> <br><b>
  <blockquote> Family, friendship, love, loyalty, protect, strength, PAIN</blockquote>
</b><br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/fighting%20redemption/lovewords_zps5146576e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390079751i/8140223._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo lovewords_zps5146576e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><b>
  <i>This is a well thought out, well put together story that gives you glimpses into the effect of being a soldier, what its like to be a family who has members that are in the SAS plus what a military wife/lover goes through when your heart is literally put on the line every time your love could be taken right away from you at any moment. <br>This story ripped open my heart, I cried full pelt sobbed, remember to breathe, tears down my face crying, but it was worth every tear seriously every single person should read this book. <br>I will say though and I give warning here I thought this was going to be a light read, I heard good things but I don't know what I was thinking, SERIOUSLY WHAT WAS I THINKING because I found myself in the midst of their story and unable to pull myself away, I couldn't concentrate on much else and I NEEDED to keep reading till I finished just so I could breathe . NO JOKE this is a phenomenal book. </i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/fighting%20redemption/cryinggif_zpsc92c03bd.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390079634ra/8140202.gif" alt=" photo cryinggif_zpsc92c03bd.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/fighting%20redemption/18B36E82-D96C-4886-B281-6D71BA3042DA_zpsa2kdvuqq.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390079634i/8140203.jpg" alt=" photo 18B36E82-D96C-4886-B281-6D71BA3042DA_zpsa2kdvuqq.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><b>So What' s it about?</b><br>When Fin was 8 and Ryan was 10 Fin stumbled over, Ryan knelt down to help being drawn to Fins unique innocent nature, upon helping Fin, Fins brother Jake wanted to know what was going on and that is where the three of them embark on a friendship. But Ryan and Fins chemistry is intense and difficult for Ryan to keep away but he does as Fin doesn't include his plan. <br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/fighting%20redemption/87EC3FF4-8EB7-4EA3-A59D-3929666C0195_zpsesh0c7gu.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390079634i/8140204._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 87EC3FF4-8EB7-4EA3-A59D-3929666C0195_zpsesh0c7gu.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/fighting%20redemption/F56853FC-B7D6-4616-98CA-7A3B5C560AD9_zpsczqtcvld.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390079634i/8140205.jpg" alt=" photo F56853FC-B7D6-4616-98CA-7A3B5C560AD9_zpsczqtcvld.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Ryan comes under the tortured hero label, he thinks he doesn't deserve to be loved, he comes from a home of abuse which is why Jake and Fins family take Ryan on as another son and as their own. He has one plan out of life and that's to become a SAS Soldier, to make a difference, to become somebody and to make his parents proud of him, he lives, breathes, dreams and wants this so he won't let Fin into his heart, he's trying to protect her. So he goes to war and Jake follows suit so Fin becomes an independent beautiful scientist. <br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/fighting%20redemption/FFD93F2B-56D8-456F-9DD2-FAAC6BFDF9D6_zpsxvs34p54.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390079634i/8140206.jpg" alt=" photo FFD93F2B-56D8-456F-9DD2-FAAC6BFDF9D6_zpsxvs34p54.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/fighting%20redemption/E2AC76DA-6F7E-458E-8C05-4030C3ABC406_zpsmvpz7uyf.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390079634i/8140207.jpg" alt=" photo E2AC76DA-6F7E-458E-8C05-4030C3ABC406_zpsmvpz7uyf.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>So years pass and they move on but eventually as they are a little older they all come back together, and that spark is still there so yes they get together, but that comes with the agony of having to live with war in their life, of the worry of having there hearts broken and this is just gut renching pain in parts, Ryan is just stubborn in parts but he is always putting Fin as number one in every decision he makes, he is her heart and hers his they struggle to survive without the other. <br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/fighting%20redemption/E79F5114-6A45-41F9-ADAE-BEF5768851A9_zpswtonomyz.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390079634i/8140208._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo E79F5114-6A45-41F9-ADAE-BEF5768851A9_zpswtonomyz.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><b>Jake</b><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/fighting%20redemption/43DD9020-3293-4A47-B547-6CBA095392FB_zps68s7ym69.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390079634i/8140209._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 43DD9020-3293-4A47-B547-6CBA095392FB_zps68s7ym69.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>I'm just going to take some time here to explain all that is Jake and what a beautiful character he is, he loves his sister like any brother would but he has a big huge heart, he's so proud of her and is her best friend in many ways. In constant contact with her, keeping her up to date with everything he's doing. Equally he loves Ryan as his brother.... they met as kids and as adults that bond is strong as ever, that's all I'm going to say here but he's one swoon worthy man, that I know you'll all love but he'll most definitely melt your heart like he did mine. <br> <br><b>
  <blockquote>"Brothers forever, right, Kindall?" Ryan grinned. "Brothers forever, Tanner."</blockquote>
</b><br> <br>So here the story continues on, moving forward, and I'm not going to tell you anything else just read it its one that needs to be experienced without much more information that I've given, but what I will say is that I have a new found love and admiration for family's in the SAS but also for military wife's that could have their worlds taken away from them at any second, that must worry constantly and for the soldiers that fight our country. I will now listen more carefully when anything comes on the news and pray for those family's to keep strong. I honestly don't know how they do it, please please read it &lt;3 <br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/fighting%20redemption/FF407D40-010E-40DF-9208-EDC953C07B0D_zpsvctozqnz.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390079634i/8140210._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo FF407D40-010E-40DF-9208-EDC953C07B0D_zpsvctozqnz.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/fighting%20redemption/48CD80A1-C2B4-4340-9BAB-C12EBEA23738_zps68ylftjz.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390079634i/8140211.jpg" alt=" photo 48CD80A1-C2B4-4340-9BAB-C12EBEA23738_zps68ylftjz.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Ryan</b><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/fighting%20redemption/45DA82FA-871D-4AD4-8E76-54F1592D0B9C_zpsl3uiofl1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390079634i/8140212._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 45DA82FA-871D-4AD4-8E76-54F1592D0B9C_zpsl3uiofl1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Finley</b><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/fighting%20redemption/7D4165A5-CFA5-4C9F-91F5-A8248E7E414F_zpswqmjekax.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390079634i/8140213._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 7D4165A5-CFA5-4C9F-91F5-A8248E7E414F_zpswqmjekax.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br> <br> And for those of you that are worried about the end and if there's an Happy HEA... the answer is <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <b>YES</b>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="13656499037808577300" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_762685178" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/762685178" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10367112-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515708587p2/10367112.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/762685178?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/10367112-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=roller-coaster-of-emotions">roller-coaster-of-emotions</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=loved">loved</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=6-star">6-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=re-read-again">re-read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=military">military</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=powerful">powerful</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer762685178" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16787777331222496656"><b> This is a 6+++ star book </b> <br/><br/><b>
  <i>" I'll love you longer than the stars that live in the sky."</i>
</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386266289ra/7325664.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><a href='http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/11225213893/' title='fightingredemption by ms.meesh, on Flickr' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386269946i/7326322.jpg' width='460' height='276' alt='fightingredemption' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/11225785103/' title='1a07efcaf7fef02aa6da8591cfc44797 by ms.meesh, on Flickr' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386272355i/7326697.jpg' width='383' height='500' alt='1a07efcaf7fef02aa6da8591cfc44797' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Before reading this book, make sure to have tissues nearby. Your heart will ache and yearn from this emotionally compelling story. I cried ugly tears but it was worth it. I can truly say that without a doubt Jake, Kyle, Ryan and Finlay have touched a part of my heart, soul and mind. Hands down Fighting Redemption is in my top 10 favorite books of 2013. <br/><br/><a href='http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/11225690824/' title='9105a68ce1b520e4a7c92df1a48f7c5c by ms.meesh, on Flickr' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386272355i/7326698.jpg' width='500' height='500' alt='9105a68ce1b520e4a7c92df1a48f7c5c' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Fighting Redemption is more than a story a</span>
  <span id="freeText16787777331222496656" style="display:none"><b> This is a 6+++ star book </b> <br><br><b>
  <i>" I'll love you longer than the stars that live in the sky."</i>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386266289ra/7325664.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/11225213893/" title="fightingredemption by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386269946i/7326322.jpg" width="460" height="276" alt="fightingredemption" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/11225785103/" title="1a07efcaf7fef02aa6da8591cfc44797 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386272355i/7326697.jpg" width="383" height="500" alt="1a07efcaf7fef02aa6da8591cfc44797" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Before reading this book, make sure to have tissues nearby. Your heart will ache and yearn from this emotionally compelling story. I cried ugly tears but it was worth it. I can truly say that without a doubt Jake, Kyle, Ryan and Finlay have touched a part of my heart, soul and mind. Hands down Fighting Redemption is in my top 10 favorite books of 2013. <br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/11225690824/" title="9105a68ce1b520e4a7c92df1a48f7c5c by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386272355i/7326698.jpg" width="500" height="500" alt="9105a68ce1b520e4a7c92df1a48f7c5c" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Fighting Redemption is more than a story about war and the men who sacrifices their lives to protect their country and freedom. It is also a story where bonds of brotherhood and friendship are formed. Lives are lost and saved. Where family is more than just blood. Where love is first found and lost, where grief and guilt can overshadow any happiness, where unspoken love speaks volumes of never-ending beautiful heartfelt love, where truths and secrets are revealed, where redemption can finally be found, where heroes are born and finally when to say goodbye and let go. <br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/11226063083/" title="d57006721da0a77e1d1487962df1f027 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386273752i/7327046.jpg" width="500" height="375" alt="d57006721da0a77e1d1487962df1f027" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/11226201796/" title="4c51d4f68a961b444f1d45aa7264a97e by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386274687i/7327228.jpg" width="456" height="500" alt="4c51d4f68a961b444f1d45aa7264a97e" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ryan Kendall grew up with a with an abusive father and a mother who neglected him till he found a second home with the Tanner family through his friendship with Jake Tanner. Ryan and Jake were inseparable; their friendship was so deep that were like brothers. Brothers who would have sacrificed and gave their life for one another. When Ryan meets Finlay, Jake’s baby sister, it was love at first sight. In his eyes, Fin was just perfect. She was the only one who had his heart. Never having told her how much he loved her, Ryan joined the SAS Army at the age of 19. Six years has past and his love for Finlay remained. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Six years, Ryan. Do you know how hurt I was, each day passing by and getting nothing-not even a note or an email? I didn't just lose you. I lost my brother too. Both of you left me, and I was okay with that. I understand that this was what you needed to do, so I moved on. I built a life that doesn't include you. That was what I had to do.”<br><br>“Why can’t I force myself to leave? I hurt too. For six years, I fought every day not to think of you, and I lost, because every day you were all I could see. You were the best thing in my life-so sweet and innocent, and so goddamn tempting… I stayed away so you could move on.”<br><br>“Don’t ever be sorry. Guilt is the only thing I can’t let you live with, baby. I won’t do that to you, even if it kills me.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/11226435153/" title="11c849dd69eb68a21a170ffc524e5bbd by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386276632i/7327788.jpg" width="500" height="500" alt="11c849dd69eb68a21a170ffc524e5bbd" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ryan and Fin’s relationship can only be described as raw, intense, fierce, palpable, and heartbreaking. Their love for each other can be felt from the first page of the prologue till the last page of the epilogue.Though their journey was never easy, Ryan and Fin, in the only way they knew how made it work. <br><br><b>
  <i>"I have a thick skin, baby...but you're under it. You're buried in there so deep it's like I was born with you in my soul. When I'm near you I'm consumed by you--your smile, your eyes, your heart. Even though we've never been together, you've always been mine, and even if I never get to keep you, you'll still be mine." </i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/11226565865/" title="359f8eb7f78e198a3211820b49ea8121 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386276632i/7327789.jpg" width="500" height="352" alt="359f8eb7f78e198a3211820b49ea8121" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Have you read a book that makes you stop and reflect on how deep and amazing these characters were? Jake, Kyle, Ryan, and Fin were fictional characters, but the way Kate McCarthy had written them, they could be easily be real. The story was so raw, honest and practically real that military families could easily relate to their story from deployment, waiting to hear if their love ones are okay, and getting that phone call or visit that will forever change your life. This book was so raw and heartfelt that every letter, every conversation, and every thoughts that Jake, Ryan and Fin exchanged played an integral part to the story-line. Ms. Kate McCarthy did a fantastic job in this book because she was able to showcase what friendship, redemption, brotherhood, family and love entails. An absolute must read! <br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/11227033315/" title="fightingRedemptionco by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386278964i/7328429.jpg" width="500" height="375" alt="fightingRedemptionco" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/933045.Kate_McCarthy" title="Kate McCarthy" rel="nofollow noopener">Kate McCarthy</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16787777331222496656" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_995886004" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/995886004" />
    <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake"><img alt="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605987751p2/11626803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/995886004?book_show_action=true">Jul 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake">Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=loved-you-since-childhood">loved-you-since-childhood</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=young-adult-new-adult">young-adult-new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=military-spec-ops">military-spec-ops</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer995886004" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9051409309555454460"><b>Strong 4.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405520894i/10409150.jpg' width='403' height='275' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I am having a hard time gathering my thoughts for this one...but that's because:<br/><br/>a) It's 0600 and my brain does not seem to be working yet. And...<br/><br/>b) I'm incredibly pissed off because I had the most awesome review EVER (well my sleep deprived mind said so for what it's worth) for this all completed, but point a resulted in me hitting delete instead of save.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405524064ra/10409574.gif' width='284' height='199' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So this is going to be a lot shorter and a lot less eloquent than I had originally intended. <br/><br/>**********************************</span>
  <span id="freeText9051409309555454460" style="display:none"><b>Strong 4.5 Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405520894i/10409150.jpg" width="403" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am having a hard time gathering my thoughts for this one...but that's because:<br><br>a) It's 0600 and my brain does not seem to be working yet. And...<br><br>b) I'm incredibly pissed off because I had the most awesome review EVER (well my sleep deprived mind said so for what it's worth) for this all completed, but point a resulted in me hitting delete instead of save.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405524064ra/10409574.gif" width="284" height="199" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So this is going to be a lot shorter and a lot less eloquent than I had originally intended. <br><br>*****************************************************************<br><br>First of all, let me start by saying that this is <b>not</b> an original story. This is a story about love and war, the dichotomy between those two entities being the foundation of stories, movies, and sonnets since...forever.<br><br>Seen this before?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405520894i/10409151._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="529" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Me too. <br><br>Now I am not here to make a political statement about war. I am here to discuss a work of <b>fiction</b>; <i>however</i>, war is not fiction and I <i>will</i> say that I believe there is an inherent beauty in the selflessness of soldiers (male and female, from <i>any</i> country) choosing to give up their homes, time with their families, and sometimes their lives to fight for their country. For their beliefs. For their families. <br><br>For the men and women in uniform standing to their left and their right. <br><br>Because that's what this book is about.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405524794i/10409779.jpg" width="346" height="363" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And I thought the author did a great job.<br><br>I really liked Finlay and Ryan. And I LOVED Jake. In fact, my favorite aspect of the story was the brotherhood between Ryan and Jake.<br><br>Also, I have and always will be a sucker for the childhood love theme. And I thought Finlay and Ryan's story was pretty epic. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405525067i/10409834.jpg" width="300" height="419" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My only complaints about this story are:<br><br>The beginning. I <b>hate it</b> when an author starts a story by revealing a major plot point<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[and in this case pretty much the ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br>And the ending. I feel like the story...lost some steam toward the conclusion. The author had built up an amazing climax. She even had me crying - which is really rare for me seeing as I am cold and heartless. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405525067ra/10409835.gif" width="499" height="259" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But instead of an awesome burst, I felt like I was left with a slowly deflating balloon. And a squeaky helium voice.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405524064i/10409575.jpg" width="500" height="332" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Overall though, I thought this was a really beautiful book about love, war, brotherhood, and the lengths to which we will go to right old wrongs...no matter how valid those wrongs may or may not be...all very timeless subjects that I thought the author weaved together to make a really beautiful story. <br><br>I would definitely recommend this to anyone who loves a classic, war themed romance novel.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405521259i/10409211._SX540_.jpg" width="540" height="325" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="9051409309555454460" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
