<div id="review_776182092" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/776182092" />
    <a title="♥Sharon♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12125670-sharon"><img alt="♥Sharon♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417537732p2/12125670.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/776182092?book_show_action=true">Nov 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Sharon♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Sharon♥" href="/user/show/12125670-sharon">♥Sharon♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer776182092" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7872739916706516328">5 ★★★★★'s!!! <br/><br/>This book really touched my heart. It was a one day read for me so that should tell you something. I loved every minute of it.<br/><br/>Fighting Redemption was such a wonderful book. It was <b>AMAZING.</b> It was <b>TOUCHING.</b> It was <b>BEAUTIFUL.</b> It was <b>EMOTIONAL.</b> Why I waited until now to read it I have no clue because it is an absolute <b>MUST READ!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/fightingredemptioncollage_zps8426a9d8.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1406666296i/10580994.jpg' alt=' photo fightingredemptioncollage_zps8426a9d8.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Okay so now that I have that out of the way let me tell you a little bit about the story. I won’t say much because I think having only a little about the s</span>
  <span id="freeText7872739916706516328" style="display:none">5 ★★★★★'s!!! <br><br>This book really touched my heart. It was a one day read for me so that should tell you something. I loved every minute of it.<br><br>Fighting Redemption was such a wonderful book. It was <b>AMAZING.</b> It was <b>TOUCHING.</b> It was <b>BEAUTIFUL.</b> It was <b>EMOTIONAL.</b> Why I waited until now to read it I have no clue because it is an absolute <b>MUST READ!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/fightingredemptioncollage_zps8426a9d8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1406666296i/10580994.jpg" alt=" photo fightingredemptioncollage_zps8426a9d8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Okay so now that I have that out of the way let me tell you a little bit about the story. I won’t say much because I think having only a little about the story in the back of your mind will allow you to experience the book better. At least I found that to be true for me.<br><br>Fighting Redemption wasn’t just a story about the men that risk their lives to protect and defend their country and freedom. And it wasn’t just a simple love story. It is so much more. It is a story about friendships, bravery and sacrifice not only in war but within family and it is a story about strength and self-respect.<br><br>The beautiful main characters in this book are Ryan Kendall, Jake Tanner and Finlay Tanner. But I also fell in love with a secondary character Kyle Brooks. I can’t put my finger on why but he crept into my heart as well. Even though he was described as being made up of “nothing but rock solid muscle” he came across as a big teddy bear. He was that guy that loved to bust balls and flirt with the ladies but he was also the guy that was there for everyone when things got tough. And things got tough.<br><br>Ryan met Jake and Finlay at the beginning of one school year. Jake and Finlay were new to the school. They were all young, Finlay being the youngest. But when Fin literally stumbles into his life there was no turning back. Finlay took hold of his heart without even knowing it. <br><br>I loved Jake. He was always so protective of Finlay and wanted her to be happy. He was such a sweetheart.<br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/Jake_zpseb1ed53b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1406666296i/10580995.jpg" alt=" photo Jake_zpseb1ed53b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And Finlay. Well she was just a simple girl. And a bit of a klutz. :) She just wanted to fall in love and live happily ever after. She was beautiful inside and out.<br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/Finlay_zps5c721416.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1406670698i/10581747.jpg" alt=" photo Finlay_zps5c721416.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The thing is, Ryan’s own family life had fallen apart. He experienced something in his young life that caused him emotional and physical pain. But it made him stronger and he became a wonderful man.<br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/Ryan_zpsf7a42c0b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1406666296i/10580997.jpg" alt=" photo Ryan_zpsf7a42c0b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Through his friendship with Jake, the Tanner’s became his new family. And from there a family bond, like no other began. The brotherly love and loyalty that grew between Jake and Ryan was something that stayed strong throughout their late teenage years and followed them through their enlistment in the SAS Army. <br><br>But Ryan’s feelings towards Finlay grew, matured and filled his heart. Ryan loved her. He wanted to protect her and always keep her safe. But he knew that his future in the service wouldn’t allow for the type of relationship she deserved so he kept his feelings tucked away. But Finlay could feel it. She knew he had feelings for her but without ever hearing those words Fin lived her life, dated and moved on.<br><br>Now six years have passed and Jake and Ryan are returning home. Time causes change and all three have changed a lot. Fin has created a life for herself with her boyfriend Ian but it isn’t a life that is complete. Hmm I wonder why that is? And Ryan, he has experience things that has tested his bravery and his mental and physical strength. But the one thing that hasn’t changed is his love for Finlay. <br><br>After their return, so much happens with Finlay, Ryan and Jake. Some of it is painful and some of it is beautiful. Their lives will never be the same be that good or bad. But what will always be a constant for them is love, friendship and the inevitability of always being part of each other’s lives.<br><br>Ryan and Finlay’s relationship was one that will grab hold of your heart and not let go. The stages they go through and what they deal with is evident that fate is playing a part in it. It wasn’t easy. But how does that quote go…. “Nothing worth having is ever easy, and all the best things in life are the result of pain. In the end, that’s what makes the good things go very great, and that’s what makes it all worth the struggle.” This is so true for them.<br><br>❤	 ❤ 	❤ 	❤<br><br>Sorry, I know I said I wouldn’t say much right….but I got carried away. If you haven’t read this book please give it a try. I <b>highly recommend</b> it. It is a story that had me thinking about things. About the families that are left behind of those that serve, about sacrifices people make and about all the good that come from all the amazing people in our armed services. ❤<br><br>I’ll leave you with one of my favorite parts in the story. Fin and Ryan are talking about when he will be leaving again and she has asked him to promise that he will be safe.<br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/fightingredemptioncollage1_zps8d1e38b8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1406666296i/10580998._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo fightingredemptioncollage1_zps8d1e38b8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“You know I can’t promise you that.” You speak to me of love, yet you’ll walk away from me so easily to go and put your life on the line! Do you know how hard that is for me?” “I’m sorry.” <br><br>Ryan pulled her around the table and into the circle of him arms. “Every piece of me is in here.” He placed his palm flat on her chest, feeling her heart beat hard and steady beneath his fingers. He closed his eyes briefly at the beauty of it. “My breath, my heart, my life. I won’t ever leave you if you if you keep that safe inside of you.” ღ</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="7872739916706516328" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_761336619" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/761336619" />
    <a title="Patrycja" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja"><img alt="Patrycja" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586460589p2/6852653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/761336619?book_show_action=true">Nov 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patrycja" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patrycja" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja">Patrycja</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer761336619" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2711865015466836046"><br/>Fighting Redemption is one of those reads that literally choke you with so many beautiful and aching emotions you can’t breath for what seems like ages. It touched me so hard, it seemed I won’t be able to think about anything else for a very long time. I really enjoyed reading Kate McCarthy’s book, because it not only took me on a wild ride through life’s obstacles and showed me amazing example of love, but made me feel, think and I just… have no words how to describe a book like this. This nove</span>
  <span id="freeText2711865015466836046" style="display:none"><br>Fighting Redemption is one of those reads that literally choke you with so many beautiful and aching emotions you can’t breath for what seems like ages. It touched me so hard, it seemed I won’t be able to think about anything else for a very long time. I really enjoyed reading Kate McCarthy’s book, because it not only took me on a wild ride through life’s obstacles and showed me amazing example of love, but made me feel, think and I just… have no words how to describe a book like this. This novel is nothing like I’ve read before, and for that I’m very grateful. It captivated me quickly with brutal honesty, raw ad gritty storyline and beautiful romance. Step by step, page by page I slowly fell in love with this complex bittersweet story.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386239135i/7318383.jpg" width="400" alt="img" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Fighting Redemption is Ryan and Finely’s story. Both of them loved each other from the time they were kids. Ryan was best friend of Jake, Finely’s brother. There were reason they buried feelings for each other and went on hurting without the other one close. <br>When Ryan joins the Army with Jake, Fin’s heart broke. Now, long years later they have the chance to finally find happiness, but there is just so many other obstacles, that maybe the happiness wasn’t written in their stars. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386239135i/7318384.png" width="400" alt="img" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It’s exceptional, gut wrenching novel. McCarthy’s done a great job in creating poignant, unforgettable, beautifully erotic tale of true love, while still fantastically picturing life of a soldier. I was astonished by how tragic and sad some things were. From time to time, my heart started beating faster and whole ‘real life’ got blurry. I was so into Ryan and Finely’s story, I wasn’t even paying attention to what was happening around me. I was hooked and then floored and then a crying mess. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386239135i/7318385._SY540_.jpg" width="400" alt="img" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Why four stars then? I don’t like reading stories written in third person point of view. This type of writing usually cheapen the experience for me. You can’t imagine how frustrating for me is loving the book but hating the third person point of view. I feel lost and not able to connect with characters more. It’s like watching TV, while I’m addicted to being one of characters. It’s hard to do so while everything is written this way: ‘she went, she thought’ and so on. So if you prefer third person point of view or it doesn’t irritate you, Fighting Redemption will be phenomenal for you. Overall, Fighting Redemption is engaging, breathtaking story that will keep you on the edge of your seat. It’s Unputdownable, good written novel that every fan of beauty, emotional roller coasters and exceptional tales of love will devour. <br><br><br><i>More reviews on <a href="http://smokinhotbookblog.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Smokin' Hot Book Blog</a> and my <a href="https://www.facebook.com/smokinhotbookblog?ref=stream&amp;hc_location=stream" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Page</a><br><br><br><br><br></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="2711865015466836046" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/778373747?book_show_action=true">Dec 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Plamena" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Plamena" href="/user/show/14813237-plamena">Plamena</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14813237-plamena?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer778373747" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17759329936088273731"><b>5 Beautiful Stars</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386239980i/7318519.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>“As long as she was here, he could run as far and as fast as he wanted, but for her he would always return.”</b>
</i><br/><br/><i>Fighting Redemption</i> is a beautiful and emotional story. A story worth remembering. A story worth reading over and over again. I loved every word. It’s because of books like this one that I love reading. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386239980i/7318520._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I was so emotional after finishing this book that I needed new days to cool off. The story touched me so deep and it felt so real.... This is the story of Ryan and Fin</span>
  <span id="freeText17759329936088273731" style="display:none"><b>5 Beautiful Stars</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386239980i/7318519.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>“As long as she was here, he could run as far and as fast as he wanted, but for her he would always return.”</b>
</i><br><br><i>Fighting Redemption</i> is a beautiful and emotional story. A story worth remembering. A story worth reading over and over again. I loved every word. It’s because of books like this one that I love reading. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386239980i/7318520._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was so emotional after finishing this book that I needed new days to cool off. The story touched me so deep and it felt so real.... This is the story of Ryan and Finlay. It’s a story of their love, friendship, pain and fighting for redemption. <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435701ra/880386.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ryan is a SAS soldier fighting in Afghanistan. Joining the army has been his dream since he was very young. Due to his dysfunctional family and an awful tragedy, Ryan is broken and needs to prove to himself that he is worthy of the redemption he seeks. So fighting for his country and helping innocent people is his way to do it. Finley and her brother (Jake) have been his family since fifth grade. And since then he has been in love with Finley. But he doesn’t have any room for mistakes... he has a goal and no one will stop him...not even the love he feels for this girl. So he leaves everything so he can pursue his dreams. <br><br>Finlay has been waiting for Ryan for six years. Granted, she tries to move on but she struggles to let go of her love for Ryan. Then he comes back and he finally wants her but it’s not that simple. It never is in life. So when they both experience one of the greatest losses in life...it’s up to them to put their broken hearts back together. And again...It won’t be easy!!! <br><br><i>
  <b>“You’re all I see. Nothing holds more beauty in my eyes than you do. No one will ever love you the way I do.”</b>
</i><br><br><br>I loved this story. I truly did! Every word got to me and I felt the pain AND the joy... It’s one of the best books I have read this year and I’m really happy I picked it up. <br><br><i>
  <b>“There are no goodbyes in life. Only see you later.”</b>
</i><br><br>I definitely recommend this story! Read it...You won’t regret it! <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17759329936088273731" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_782154965" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/782154965" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/782154965?book_show_action=true">Dec 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=cry-baby-books">cry-baby-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer782154965" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2490162173742830671"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“Why did everyone always paint love as pretty rainbows and happily ever afters? It wasn't any of that. To love was to feel the greatest of agony, burn in the hottest fires of hell and fail the only people who mattered."</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388762432i/7923002._SX540_.jpg' width='390' height='480' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I’m not a huge fan of third person pov writing, but this story was well written, well paced and I actually read it in one sitting and was left with a big smile on my face once I finished.<br/><br/>I did however struggle with my feelings for Ryan for most of the book and was on </span>
  <span id="freeText2490162173742830671" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“Why did everyone always paint love as pretty rainbows and happily ever afters? It wasn't any of that. To love was to feel the greatest of agony, burn in the hottest fires of hell and fail the only people who mattered."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388762432i/7923002._SX540_.jpg" width="390" height="480" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I’m not a huge fan of third person pov writing, but this story was well written, well paced and I actually read it in one sitting and was left with a big smile on my face once I finished.<br><br>I did however struggle with my feelings for Ryan for most of the book and was on the fence on whether Ryan deserved Finlay at all. I mean he didn’t do anything with feelings for years. Write her a note, give her a call do something! He was very good at walking away and made it seem so easy <b>BUT</b> that did give him a real feel and he battled his own demons and fears. I found him so frustrating but I think that was the idea of the story on some level to rejoice when he finally got his act together.<br><br>My reasons for not fully 5 starring this one:<br><br>I think at some point in their childhood there should have been a special moment or something that showed their connection. Something swoon worthy or unforgettable.<br><br>I loved the supporting characters as much as the main characters, Jake, Rachel and Kyle were just fantastic.<br><br>This is definitely a story that has me still thinking about it long after I read the last page.<br><br>Overall, a good read that I would recommend because Ryan and Finlay definitely worked when all was said and done. <br><br>Job Well Done Kate McCarthy!<br><br><b>
  <i>“I’ll love you longer than the stars that live in the sky.”</i>
</b><br></span>

<div id="review_812106439" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/812106439" />
    <a title="M. ~ B&amp;B" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14479657-m-b-b"><img alt="M. ~ B&amp;B" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435261660p2/14479657.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/812106439?book_show_action=true">Jan 04, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="M. ~ B&amp;B" class="user" itemprop="url" name="M. ~ B&amp;B" href="/user/show/14479657-m-b-b">M. ~ B&amp;B</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer812106439" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14032804436534843590">My issue with this book, and many other books too, is that they're all so much alike. It's just so standard, that I guessed pretty much all of what happened. Even Ryan's huge secret that made him self-destruct and run away to become a soldier wasn't a surprise to me. <br/><br/>I understand that almost everything has already been tried before and authors are bound to work with the same themes and events. That's fine though, as long as the execution is amazing, I can get over the unoriginality. However, the</span>
  <span id="freeText14032804436534843590" style="display:none">My issue with this book, and many other books too, is that they're all so much alike. It's just so standard, that I guessed pretty much all of what happened. Even Ryan's huge secret that made him self-destruct and run away to become a soldier wasn't a surprise to me. <br /><br />I understand that almost everything has already been tried before and authors are bound to work with the same themes and events. That's fine though, as long as the execution is amazing, I can get over the unoriginality. However, the execution of Fighting Redemption was just okay. I didn't feel any connection between the love couple, I didn't feel connected to any of the main characters and, to me, it felt like their actions didn't make any sense.<br /><br />I love a good build-up to a relationship, but when an author decides to skip the build-up, start in the middle, and explain by flashbacks, I want the flashbacks to be powerful. I felt like the flashbacks in this story lacked power completely. From the flashbacks, I got the impression that Fin and Ryan were really good, close friends, and none of them ever tried to be more. When they reunited after six years, suddenly they were spilling their hearts over how hurt they are, how much they missed the other and how they just cannot be. I just feel like I missed the boat on their relationship. And when they do finally admit all this, they just keeping running around in circles. I thought Ryan was stupid. Fin annoyed me in the beginning too. I wanted to punch both at some points. And my lack of tolerance had everything to do with the lack of connection. <br /><br />Also, I felt a lot of it was repetitive and some of the dialogue was cheesy. They always kissed until they had to catch their breath, or until one of them was breathless. And there was a big emphasize on Ryan being possessive and alpha in the bedroom and I was like, whatever the author/Ryan is trying too hard. Now that I think of it, the characters felt hollow to me, like silhouettes. The only ones that showed some color were Kyle and Jake.<br /><br />The only war story that I have read that <i>really</i> shows the effect war has on soldiers and the ones left behind, is <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17381391.In_the_Stillness" title="In the Stillness by Andrea Randall" rel="nofollow noopener">In The Stillness</a>. That story was so powerful and realistic. I cried every time I read a flashback in that book and the story was just so emotion-driven. No excuses, no dark pasts, no abuses, just plain, real, unapologetic <i>pain</i>. The author managed to take a theme that's been used a lot and still make it original.<br /><br />Sorry, I'm such an asshole for talking about another book in my review for this book. I'm just gonna finish this review by saying I gave this three stars, because I felt indifferent towards it. It wasn't bad, just nothing that got my heart racing and nothing that hasn't been done before.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14032804436534843590" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer722579168" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2434120312438661004"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389902753i/8090650._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389901447i/8090100._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Oh my goodness!! Wow!<br/><br/>Yeh, that just about sums up my feelings right about now.<br/>This book is absolutely stunning. You <i>have</i> to read this!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389901447i/8090101._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>5+ Stars for Ryan & Fin!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389901447i/8090102._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Oh God. This book did a number on me. I was a mess. I'm still a mess! <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099889._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Ryan Kendall first laid eyes on Finlay Tanner when she was just ten years old, and she was eight. He fast became inseparable with Finlay's brother, Jake and all but moved in with their family to escape the cruel hands of his abusive, alcoholic father and the devastation t</span>
  <span id="freeText2434120312438661004" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389902753i/8090650._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389901447i/8090100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh my goodness!! Wow!<br><br>Yeh, that just about sums up my feelings right about now.<br>This book is absolutely stunning. You <i>have</i> to read this!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389901447i/8090101._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>5+ Stars for Ryan &amp; Fin!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389901447i/8090102._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh God. This book did a number on me. I was a mess. I'm still a mess! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385215295i/7099889._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ryan Kendall first laid eyes on Finlay Tanner when she was just ten years old, and she was eight. He fast became inseparable with Finlay's brother, Jake and all but moved in with their family to escape the cruel hands of his abusive, alcoholic father and the devastation that ruled his household. <br>As Jake and Ryan grew older, they made plans to join the army. For Ryan, it was a way of escaping and ultimately proving that he could be somebody. As Ryan, Jake and Fin matured through their teenage years, Ryan became increasingly aware of his feelings for Fin, but always knew that he would never be able give her what she deserved and in the end, he knew he would have to leave her, to go to war.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>The Army, and the war, owned him - body and soul. Fin never stood a chance.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389901447i/8090103._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But as a huge part of each others lives, Fin and Ryan's paths cross as time passes and their lives move on. An avoidable connection, tragic circumstances, shared sorrow and a bond that rooted itself deeply in each of them as children makes staying away from one another impossible. <br>Can Ryan allow himself to be the man that Fin needs and deserves, or can Fin stand to fall for with the tormented, broken, guilt ridden soldier that she has always loved?<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>What if love wasn't enough for them? Would it heal the deep lacerations life had placed on his heart, or would he always be so completely broken that he would never fully be hers?</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I've read Kate McCarthy's work before. I read and loved <i>Give Me Love</i> and I have <i>Give Me Strength</i> on my Kindle waiting to be read. So when she asked me to take a look at <i>Fighting for Redemption</i> I almost bit her hand off. I'd heard great things about the book, not least of all that Ryan Kendall had just been crowned 'Sexiest Soldier' in my Smitten's Book Awards 2013, so I couldn't wait to dive in. I naughtily whizzed it to the top of my TBR pile and off I went. Well... Kate absolutely blew me away!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389901447i/8090104._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is heartbreaking. <i>Truly</i> heartbreaking. It's a total 'ugly-cry' candidate. Face-goosebumps, snotty nose, stomach ache, the whole hog! I absolutely sobbed my heart out at numerous points. One part in particular was just excruciating. It's so emotionally heartfelt and evocative. I really <i>felt</i> every single word with everything in me. It's one of those that takes over your life while you're reading it. Functioning goes out of the window and it's just better for everyone if you get the book read so that you can resume some semblance of your normal self. You've all been there. Well, <i>Fighting Redemption</i> is one of those.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I'll love you longer than the stars that live in the sky."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>So, it kicks off with a beautifully heart aching prologue that will give you a little panic attack. I have to admit, this did make me hyperventilate slightly and I did just have to check that I wasn't reading a book that'd leave me bleeding raw emotion all over the carpet at the end with no chance of survival. Don't worry. Rest assured, this book <i>does</i> have the perfect happy ending. So now we've cleared that up...<br><br>I <i>love</i> the characters. The character development is superb. We get a great insight in the childhoods of Ryan and Fin, as they grow, mature, become aware of their attraction to one another, try to fight it, follow their dreams, etc. etc. Kate McCarthy ensures that you fall in love over the years, with each adorable moment, teasing touch and stolen glance, just as Fin and Ryan do. I felt like I really <i>knew</i> these characters; a sure fire way to engage a reader. And I just could not put this book down. In fact, I finished it at 3.30am this morning, do I am a super sleepy Smitten today! But it was so worth it.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389901447i/8090105._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Fin is a great leading lady. She's smart, gorgeous, ordinary, a little gawky, a tad awkward and I absolutely adore her relationship with her brother Jake, who we will chat more about in a sec. Fin is two years younger than Ryan and it's clear she idolises him. It's sooo sweet to read. Her heart breaks when Ryan and Jake go off to war and I really felt her pain. But I loved that she had her own ambitions and dreams and that she made sure she carved out a great future for herself.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I'd have given you my entire heart if you'd only asked, but it's not yours now. It's not yours."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I don't even know where to begin with Ryan. One of my favourite book characters ever. Seriously. This guy is book-boyfriend gold! He's so heavily weighed down with his past and it's frustrating as hell, but oh my goodness you just want to scoop him up and cuddle him better. He has a beautiful heart and absolutely worships both Jake and Fin. And let's not forget that he is sexy as <i>hell</i>!! He's a muscle bound, tanned, ripped, tattooed army <i>GOD</i>! *fans self* I can't even... *wipes drool from chin*<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389901447i/8090106.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Stop trying to be a hero all the time. You're so busy saving everyone else you forget about yourself."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I love how much he wants Fin. Scratch that, he <i>needs</i> Fin! It's insanely sexy. The sexual tension is delicious. I love it; that but that makes you scream 'Get together already' at your Kindle, when in reality, it's the fact that they're teasing and enticing you that makes it all the more scrumptious! But that tipping point, when he decides nothing is going to get in his way any longer... Squeeee... *claps hands* I was so there. So in those moments, cheering him on. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389901447i/8090107.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I want you, Fin," he finally admitted. "So much I can't sleep from it. I lie in bed at night and I dream of my lips on yours, my mouth tasting every inch of you. I want to fuck you until I go blind from it and even then I don't think it would ever be enough."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>And as Fin and Ryan's relationship develops, there are so many scenes that just melted me inside. It's intimate, intense, tragic, romantic and there's a sense of desperation that tugs at your heart-strings. I've got the most gorgeous feeling right now, a mix of longing and warmth.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I have thick skin baby, but you're under it. You're burned in there so deep it's like I was born with you in my soul. When I'm near you I'm consumed by you - your smile, your eyes, your heart. Even though we've never been together, you've always been mine, and even if I never get to keep you, you'll still be mine."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I can't write this review without giving a very special mention (and a face) to the best brother ever, Jake Tanner! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389901447i/8090108._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What a cutie!! Again, he's a hunky army hottie with a great, fun, confident, cheeky attitude. Jake and Fin are very close and it's so lovely. He's the protective, loving, funny older brother that we all wish we had. His relationship with Ryan is heart warming too. Ryan has so little in his life of any worth and Jake just totally makes up for all of that! They really are brothers in every sense of the word other than blood. In every way that matters. Jake plays a massive part in this story. He's the glue between Ryan and Fin, he's the voice of reason, he's the relief in dark, heavy situations. Be warned; You'll fall almost as head-over-heels for Jake as you will for Ryan. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"There are no goodbyes in life. Only see you later."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>And did I mention that these sexy so-and-so's are also Australian?? So all of this is wrapped up with a swoonworthy Aussie drawl! And yeh, I totally read the whole thing in that sexy accent, too! Hey, it sounds great in my head!<br><br>Obviously this book is about the life of a soldier and the loved ones they leave behind. Honestly, I have <i>no</i> idea how the military wives do it. I cannot begin to imagine how it feels to stand and watch your man board a plane to take him off to the uncertainty of war. Because it broke my freakin' heart just to read it. I truly have the utmost admiration for the men who serve our countries <i>and</i> the women who wait for them at home. Jeez, what a painful, terrifying life.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Don't go lusting after a soldier, Rachael. They're not good for your health."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389901447i/8090109._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is so much I can't mention, because I really don't want to spoil anything for anybody. But there's a lot to this story. You will go through so many different emotions and highs and lows. I so want every single person on my friends list to read this book, because I want to have late night heart-to-hearts about how wonderful Ryan Kendall is. <br><i>Fighting Redemption</i> moved me on so many levels. This is one of those books that I will think about and lovingly sigh over in months/years to come. I know it. And <i>those</i> are the books that everybody needs to read.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389960074i/8113219._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And now I am off to give everybody dear to me a huge great big hug, because that it was what Fin and Ryan's story has done to me!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389901447i/8090110._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389733166i/8051760._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><i>Fighting Redemption</i> Statistics</b><br><b>• Steam Rating (out of 5):</b> ♥♥♥♥<br><b>• Ending:</b> HEA<br><b>• Length:</b> 346 pages<br><b>• Narrative:</b> Alternates between Ryan and Fin's POVs. Third person. Past tense.<br><b>• Series:</b> ✗ <br><b>• Can this be read as a standalone?</b> Yes<br><b>• Themes:</b><br>War<br>Tortured hero<br>Childhood friends<br><b>• WARNING. This book includes...</b> <br>Sexual content. Death. Scenes of war.<br><b>• Writing:</b> Fantastic<br><br>Check out this review on my blog ➜ <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/2014/01/16/fighting-redemption-by-kate-mccarthy-%E2%9C%B0%E2%9C%B0%E2%9C%B0%E2%9C%B0%E2%9C%B0/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com...</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389786435i/8054383._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/Fighting-Redemption-Kate-McCarthy-ebook/dp/B00H1BIZDU/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1389901216&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=fighting+redemption" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756313._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Fighting-Redemption-Kate-McCarthy-ebook/dp/B00H1BIZDU/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1389901216&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=fighting+redemption" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392852i/756314._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Like this review and want to keep up to date with more book news…?</b><br><blockquote>Follow me at the links below…</blockquote><br>My blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a><br>Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/SmittensBookBlog">https://www.facebook.com/SmittensBook...</a></span>

  <i>"For six years I fought every day not to think of you, and I lost, because every day you were all I could see."</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/tumblr_mbtdmnNMUP1qlxnhco6_250_zps3e328cec.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386621730ra/7406917.gif" alt="LOL photo tumblr_mbtdmnNMUP1qlxnhco6_250_zps3e328cec.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ryan still doesn't think he is good enough for her and wants her to move on with her life.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/tumblr_m1rrraTyjS1qcc73io1_500_zpsfbeb169b.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>But will Finlay move on with her life or try to stay with Ryan and help him battle his demons, or will she eventually wind up by herself anyway?<br><br><b>
  <i>"It doesn't matter if you live a billion years, or just a short handful. It's how bright you burn while living that really matters."</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY/tumblr_lyc52n7FaU1qak4zoo1_500_large_zps5aa41368.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Oh and FYI you will at least tear up in this book. If you don't, you probably don't have a soul. ;)<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/real-house-wives-you-should-know-gif_zps1ded8347.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_754950009" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/754950009" />
    <a title="❥ KAT ❥ Kitty Kats Crazy About Books" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6245313-kat-kitty-kats-crazy-about-books"><img alt="❥ KAT ❥ Kitty Kats Crazy About Books" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1582051737p2/6245313.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/754950009?book_show_action=true">Nov 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="❥ KAT ❥ Kitty Kats Crazy About Books" class="user" itemprop="url" name="❥ KAT ❥ Kitty Kats Crazy About Books" href="/user/show/6245313-kat-kitty-kats-crazy-about-books">❥ KAT ❥ Kitty Kats Crazy About Books</a>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">

  <span id="freeText2655634747067730802" style="display:none"><b>5 staggering "Ryan" stars</b> ARC<br><br>My review plus others can be seen on my Facebook page (<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://tinyurl.com/mg95ecm">http://tinyurl.com/mg95ecm</a>)<br><br>I've just finished this and it feels like all my emotions have been put through the wringer and spat out, this book will make you laugh, cry, you'll feel moments of anger you name it, you will feel it!!<br><br>Saying I loved this book is an understatement, I devoured it, it consumed me!!<br><br>Ryan's always dreamt of being a soldier just like his grandfather, he'd been ten years old when it had taken root in his head,even at that age his dream of being a soldier had already taken hold in his soul.<br><br>Life at home for Ryan was a nightmare, his dad was an asshole and a drunk, becoming a soldier would be Ryan's escape plan and something he had to focus on..<br><br>That was until Fin stumbled into his life and he nearly lost focus of that goal..A strong bond of friendship forms between Ryan, Finlay and her brother Jake is breathtakingly beautiful, they became fast friends..<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=jab5s3" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><i>"Six years, Ryan, do you know how hurt I was, each day passing by and not even a note or an email? I didn't just lose you, I lost my brother too, both of you left me, but I was ok with that, I understood that this was what you needed to do, so I moved on."</i><br><br><i>"I'd have given you my entire heart if only you'd only asked, but you never did, but it's not yours now."</i><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2yydnb6" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_690681610" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/690681610" />
    <a title="Tammy  Zautner" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6539323-tammy-zautner"><img alt="Tammy  Zautner" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1461189789p2/6539323.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/690681610?book_show_action=true">Aug 09, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tammy  Zautner" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tammy  Zautner" href="/user/show/6539323-tammy-zautner">Tammy  Zautner</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6539323-tammy-zautner?shelf=6-stars">6-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6539323-tammy-zautner?shelf=worthy-reads-of-2013">worthy-reads-of-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer690681610" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9554564223465308808"><b>6 HUGE STARS</b><br/><br/>This is a story about war and the cost of sacrifice. Where bonds are formed, and friendships found. Where those who are strong, fall hard. Where love is let go, heartache is born, and heroes are made. Where one man learns that the hardest fight of all is the fight to save himself.<br/><br/>"The Army and the SAS had been his dream--his chance to be somebody, save lives, show his parents he was worth something. Being a soldier had been his escape, his flight from the demons that bound him. War i</span>
  <span id="freeText9554564223465308808" style="display:none"><b>6 HUGE STARS</b><br /><br />This is a story about war and the cost of sacrifice. Where bonds are formed, and friendships found. Where those who are strong, fall hard. Where love is let go, heartache is born, and heroes are made. Where one man learns that the hardest fight of all is the fight to save himself.<br /><br />"The Army and the SAS had been his dream--his chance to be somebody, save lives, show his parents he was worth something. Being a soldier had been his escape, his flight from the demons that bound him. War is a cold, selfish bitch. It changes you. It makes you hard, and it makes you hurt, yet somehow, we keep going back for more."<br /><br />I'll be the first to admit, I am a bit biased, as I beta read this stunningly beautiful story of war and its aftermath. However, I'm not reviewing this book as its beta reader, I am reviewing it as a huge fan of Kate McCarthy's. What I love the most about her is her uncanny ability to write one hell of an addictive love story that you feel with every breath you take and live with every turn of the page, that is just one of the many reasons I am such a huge fan of hers.<br /><br />"Would they only ever have those fleeting moments—the ones where you lived the briefest, loved the hardest, and burned like the devil had set fire to your very soul? They were the only moments in his life that had been worth a damn."<br /><br />Fighting Redemption is the epitome of powerful; the gamut of emotions you'll experience will leave you aching in ways I can’t even begin to describe. I want you to prepare for the fact that your heart will be sitting huddled somewhere in the corner of your stomach for at least 75% of this book. Let us also not forget that you’ll barely be able to breathe, or even contain the ability to see through the tears freely sobbing down your face. Fighting Redemption is the newest emotional thrill ride coming soon to an e-reader near you. I strongly suggest you buckle in and hold on tight. Unless you're one of those oh so fearless types who like to test their courage and ride the ride with their hands thrown in the air, at that point there’s nothing else I can tell you, other than don't say I didn't warn you. I promise even with holding on to those bars you’ll still experience a rush. Please don't dismiss it lightly when I tell you, you’re about to experience, one hell of, an intense emotional roller coaster ride.<br /><br />"Why did everyone always paint love as pretty rainbows and happily ever afters? It wasn't any of that. To love was to feel the greatest of agony, burn in the hottest fires of hell and fail the only people who mattered."<br /><br />Ryan and Fin's relationship is a gut wrenching and heart-breaking tale, that will not only transport you to another world, it will hold you captive from the very first page. Our hero and heroine are gritty, raw and beyond captivating; their connection a beautiful blend of chemistry and frustration. Their two worlds colliding and exploding as they struggle to deal with tragedy, inner demons, mistakes, love, loss, forgiveness, and redemption. These two have to work double hard to overcome the hellish obstacles life has thrown at them, in order to experience even the tiniest slice of heaven. Nothing about this duo was easy, everything in their lives has come at a price, and that price was so damn steep. There wasn't a moment throughout their journey that Ryan and Fin weren't ripping my heart out with their intense depth, love, and emotions.<br /><br />"I have a thick skin, baby...but you're under it. You're buried in there so deep it's like I was born with you in my soul. When I'm near you I'm consumed by you--your smile, your eyes, your heart. Even though we've never been together, you've always been mine, and even if I never get to keep you, you'll still be mine."<br /><br />Alas, just when you think you can lean back and settle in all comfy like (I’d like to be able to say there isn't that much more hell Kate could put us through, but…), I'm here to warn you that’s not even remotely close to being a possibility. Stop, I can already tell you want to be brave and loosen your grip!! Do not drop those hands, keep holding on tight to those bars. I promise they are there for your safety, as well as the safety of your e-reader. Kate is pure evil, I tell you, and she isn't anywhere close to being done with utterly and completely wrecking you! This is an author who has no qualms about slowly twisting your heart into tiny little pieces that hurt so excruciatingly bad that you think you may just pass out from the pain; then and only then does she decide you've held on long enough and can begin the mending process.<br /><br />“I’d give almost anything to wake up to that every morning.”<br />“Almost anything.” She backed up a step. “That’s always been our problem, hasn't it?”<br /><br />This book is by far my number one read this year. FR is Kate McCarthy at her BEST. Ryan, Jake, Fin, and Kyle will be with me for years to come, as these characters invaded every ounce of my heart, soul, and mind. I know without a doubt that this book will go down as an ultimate favorite of mine. Kate has proved herself time and time again to be a gifted author. Fighting Redemption has her heart and soul laid bare on every page, with every single word. She's set the bar high, and I, for one, am wicked proud to be one of the first people who had the chance to experience the beauty of Ryan and Fin from day one.<br /><br />Hands down a 6 star read for me!<br /><br />P.S. Don't forget to buy stock in Kleenex.<br /><br />Thanks to Kate McCarthy for providing me a beta copy and arc in exchange for an honest review.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9554564223465308808" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_779639795" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/779639795" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/779639795?book_show_action=true">Dec 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=sob-fest">sob-fest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=soldier">soldier</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=war">war</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=omg-romantic">omg-romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=brother-best-friend">brother-best-friend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pb-i-own-signed">pb-i-own-signed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer779639795" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12190540314980855455"><b><i>“You’re all I see. Nothing holds more beauty in my eyes than you do. No one will ever love you the way I do.”</i><br/><br/>Oh. My. God. What an incredible, intensely emotional story!</b> Not only is it a beautiful, heart-wrenching romance, but it’s also a story about the love of family – both made and chosen, the bonds between brothers, and the sacrifices made by those who choose to fight for others. <br/><br/>Fin and Ryan have loved each other since their childhood. The best friend of Fin’s older brother, Jake, Ryan pract</span>
  <span id="freeText12190540314980855455" style="display:none"><b><i>“You’re all I see. Nothing holds more beauty in my eyes than you do. No one will ever love you the way I do.”</i><br /><br />Oh. My. God. What an incredible, intensely emotional story!</b> Not only is it a beautiful, heart-wrenching romance, but it’s also a story about the love of family – both made and chosen, the bonds between brothers, and the sacrifices made by those who choose to fight for others. <br /><br />Fin and Ryan have loved each other since their childhood. The best friend of Fin’s older brother, Jake, Ryan practically lived in their house, trying desperately to escape his own family. Through the years they were close and were always there for each other, but Ryan never felt worthy of Fin, so even though they both knew there was something special between them, neither of them ever acted on it. <br /><br />Having dreamed of being a soldier for as long as he can remember, Ryan and Jake enlist with the Australian Army, and the two of them become members of the SAS (special forces) and are sent to fight in Afghanistan. Six years later, they have returned home after their fourth tour, and upon seeing each other for the first time in six years, the chemistry between Fin and Ryan, which has only increased over the years, explodes.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I want you, Fin,” he finally admitted. “So damn much I can’t sleep from it. I lie in bed at night and I dream of my lips on yours, my mouth tasting every inch you. I want to fuck you until I go blind from it and even then I don’t think it would ever be enough.”<br /> <br />“For six years I fought every day not to think of you, and I lost, because every day you were all I could see. You were the best thing in my life”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />Just… wow. The emotion and the UST between these two is off the freaking charts! You can feel every little moment, and I was bouncing up and down in my chair and squeeing with glee! But there are a lot of things standing in their way. And with their careers, relationships, issues from the past, fear for the future, and the reality of both of their lives to overcome, it’s far from an easy road for either of them<br /><br />I feel like anything else that I say about the storyline is going to sound cliché, but it’s absolutely not, and there’s no way I can do the story justice. You need to read it and just take it all in as it unfolds, because it’s an amazing story. Both beautifully romantic and horribly devastating, it’s one of those books that you don’t just read, you experience.<br /><br />The relationship between Fin and Ryan is absolutely incredible. The love that they have for each other is so strong, and I felt every moment along with them. The longing, the heartbreak, the passion, the huge highs and the devastating lows. They go through so much in this story, and at times it’s really hard reading, and yes, I read with tears streaming down my face. But there are also lots of happy (and steamy) times, and I loved seeing them together! And through it all, there is never any doubting their love for each other, and every single moment is beautiful. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I have a thick skin, baby … but you’re under it. You’re buried in there so deep it’s like I was born with you in my soul … When I’m near you I’m consumed by you — your smile, your eyes, your heart. Even though we’ve never been together, you’ve always been mine, and even if I never get to keep you, you’ll still be mine.” <br /><br />“Every piece of me is in here.” He placed his palm flat on her chest, feeling her heart beat hard and steady beneath his fingers. He closed his eyes briefly at the beauty of it. “My breath, my heart, my life. I won’t ever leave you if you keep that safe inside of you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />Of course there was never any doubt that I would fall in love with Ryan. He’s brave, strong, loving and loyal. I loved the way the author explored his commitment to his career, and his heartfelt need to help others, doing it without question and with such devotion. You have to respect him for that. He’s also got a huge heart, and although he is emotionally damaged, he is absolutely crazy about his girl. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b><i>“Christ. He didn’t just love her, he fucking </i>adored<i> her. He’d give his life for her if he had to.”</i></b>
</blockquote><br /><br />And Fin more than holds her own against him. She’s intelligent, she’s sensible, and she knows what she wants and isn’t afraid to reach out and grab it. She shows amazing strength in all that she goes through, and I love that she’s strong enough to put herself out there for Ryan and be there for him when she knows he needs her.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “You’re the strongest person I’ve ever known, but someone smart and brave once told me that it’s always the strongest that fall the hardest. You can trust me, Ryan. Let go. I’ll be here to catch you. I’ll always be here.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />Throughout the book there is a very strong focus on relationships, and I loved how the author explored that. Not only between Fin and Ryan, but also their relationships with Jake. Fin has a beautiful relationship with her brother, and Jake and Ryan’s bond is amazing. I loved the scenes with them all together. <br /><br />The other characters also bring a lot to the story, and I love the relationships and how they all interplay, particularly with Kyle, Rachael, Fin and Jake’s parents, and the boys in Ryan and Jake’s squad (the banter between these guys is sensational!). The bonds are all really strong, and I love the way that they all have each other’s backs, but they’re not afraid to pull out the punches when needed.<br /><br />Through war and tragedy, love and life, Fin and Ryan’s story unfolds with incredible emotion. It's one of those books that's written in a way that you can see it all playing out in front of you like a movie, with the dual POV letting you know exactly what they are both feeling, and it's so beautifully done. I felt so connected to these characters (possibly helped along by the fact that they are living in my home town, which was a surprising bonus!), and I was mesmerized from start to finish. It broke my heart over and over, only to patch it up and have me swooning soon after. The story is an incredible journey and I absolutely loved it - and yes, there is a HEA. <br /><br />5 stars.<br /><br /><br />On a side note - I can’t even begin to imagine what the families of soldiers go through with their loved ones so far from home and facing death every day. They must be so proud, but to live with so much fear has to be truly horrific. I witnessed a small piece of it here, and my heart goes out to all of those who sacrifice so much for the sake of others, and to those who love them. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I know the final scene of this book is going to be one that stays with me forever. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12190540314980855455" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer14842003469061519850">3.5 -4 ★'s <br/><br/><i>"I'll love you longer than the stars that live in the sky." </i><br/><br/>I'm just going to premise this review by saying I am not a fan of military type stories. I know, <i>I know</i>...then why the hell did I read it? Well, for the angst of course, but I should've known better because there's always a certain plot line that's in these stories...~sigh~<br/><br/>However, as you can see by the 3.5 - 4 star rating that I did enjoy the story. Ryan and Finlay are wonderful and sweet together even though you are going t</span>
  <span id="freeText14842003469061519850" style="display:none">3.5 -4 ★'s <br><br><i>"I'll love you longer than the stars that live in the sky." </i><br><br>I'm just going to premise this review by saying I am not a fan of military type stories. I know, <i>I know</i>...then why the hell did I read it? Well, for the angst of course, but I should've known better because there's always a certain plot line that's in these stories...~sigh~<br><br>However, as you can see by the 3.5 - 4 star rating that I did enjoy the story. Ryan and Finlay are wonderful and sweet together even though you are going to want to hit Ryan over the head a few times. <br><br>They meet when Ryan is twelve and Finlay is ten. He is instantly drawn to her but he becomes best friends with her brother, Jake. That doesn't stop him from wanting her unfortunately he has something he wants even more and that's to be a soldier. It pretty much colors every aspect in his life. <br><br>He never acts on his feelings for Finlay and then him and Jake are off to the Australian Army and are gone for six years. It was a bit to take in that he never even wrote her in all that time. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398399054ra/9409892.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Finlay wants Ryan just as much as he wants her but make no mistake about it, she's not waiting around forever. In fact, she dates in high school and then has a pretty serious boyfriend (Ian) by the time Ryan does come home. <br><br>Things are little intense when that happens because Finlay and Jake have bought a house together and that's where Ryan is staying. And let me just say that the sexual chemistry is off the charts! But remember what I said about knocking Ryan in the head? Yea, you're gonna want to do that a few times. <br><br>Then "that" plot line happens and yes, it's emotional, but I just hate it. It just made everything that much worse for these two but at least it gives them the final push that they needed. And for a while...things were just peachy, it just didn't last. <br><br>From the prologue, you have an idea of what's going to happen next. It took some crazy drama for Ryan to finally figure things out but thankfully, it happened.<br><br>♦ BTW...we really need a book about Kyle and Rachael!</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13834386031108565388"><i>I won the ARC Giveaway! Via <a href='http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/?zx=2c7d1b1b73a25e3d' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a><br/></i><br/><br/><b>5 touchingly beautiful stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384490731i/6887241._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Ryan Kendall’s life changed the day he saw Finlay Tanner; the need to protect her instant. And the bond of friendship that forms between Ryan, Finlay and her brother Jake is one that knows no end. <br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “All of a sudden she smiled, wide, vibrant. The way it lit up her face drew the attention of those around her. It was like you’d been given the gift of seeing the sun radiate brilliant rays through dark clouds.</b></i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText13834386031108565388" style="display:none"><i>I won the ARC Giveaway! Via <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/?zx=2c7d1b1b73a25e3d" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a><br></i><br><br><b>5 touchingly beautiful stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384490731i/6887241._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Ryan Kendall’s life changed the day he saw Finlay Tanner; the need to protect her instant. And the bond of friendship that forms between Ryan, Finlay and her brother Jake is one that knows no end. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “All of a sudden she smiled, wide, vibrant. The way it lit up her face drew the attention of those around her. It was like you’d been given the gift of seeing the sun radiate brilliant rays through dark clouds.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Ryan had only wanted one thing his entire life, to escape and to be a soldier. It was his escape plan and the only way he knew how to silent the ghost of his past. But the way he felt for Finlay wasn’t something that was erased with the six years since he said goodbye.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384490731i/6887242.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Ryan and Jake are stationed in Afghanistan, two soldiers who may not share the same blood, but are still brothers in every way. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384490731i/6887243.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>When they are set to return home Ryan is coming face to face with the girl he left all those years ago. The one girl that he has never let go.<br><br>Fin fell in love with a boy that became a soldier, a man dedicating to protecting and sacrificing himself for the ones he loved. So she lived her life, for six year she tried to let go of the dream of the man she loved, a man that would always be leaving. But when she welcomes him and her brother home, living under the same roof might just prove to be a temptation far too great to resist.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1384490731i/6887244._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “You came home and God help me, I’m so relived you’re here that it burns me from the inside out.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><i> Kate McCarthy’s Fighting Redemption was a powerful and moving story that exceeded the realm of romance. This was about war, the unbreakable bond that is formed, the feeling of looming loss that weighs down the hearts of those standing at the airbase waiving their goodbyes and this is about healing the scars of the past so that you can have a future. <br><br>A broken hero, childhood friends, war, loss, pain, healing and love. This was everything all rolled into one fantastic story. I <br><br>I bawled like a baby. Plain and simple. Completely shameless as I read this book with vision blurred with tears. I felt like my heart was ripped out and shoved back into my chest. Stories about war are just one of those things that hits you hard. Even if you don’t have love ones serving, it’s just one of those things that moves you. Kate McCarthy did an amazing job portraying the sacrifice of those that serve their country and how that affects those that they must leave behind to do so.<br><br>There were so many moments in this story that crushed me in that good way that just makes you smile at how much it hurts. </i> <b>This was an unputdownable book. </b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13834386031108565388" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44137919-mikee-readwithmikee"><img alt="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583262285p2/44137919.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1721089744?book_show_action=true">Aug 06, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mikee (ReadWithMikee)" href="/user/show/44137919-mikee-readwithmikee">Mikee (ReadWithMikee)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44137919-mikee-readwithmikee?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1721089744" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14881697986420813615">Find me on <a href='http://www.instagram.com/readwithmikee' rel='nofollow noopener'>Instagram</a> & <a href='http://www.twitter.com/readwithmikee' rel='nofollow noopener'>Twitter</a>!<br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>❝That’s how I remember you. But you’re not looking at me like that now, and I need you to do that. I need you to wake up and smile at me like I’m your everything, because without you, I’m not anyone’s anything.❞</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Okay so I decided to spontaneously pick this up and I'm honestly surprised at how much I actually enjoyed this. I've been searching for a storyline similar to this and I'm glad I found it in Fighting Redemption.<br/><br/>This book is far from perfect. It i</span>
  <span id="freeText14881697986420813615" style="display:none">Find me on <a href="http://www.instagram.com/readwithmikee" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> &amp; <a href="http://www.twitter.com/readwithmikee" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a>!<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>❝That’s how I remember you. But you’re not looking at me like that now, and I need you to do that. I need you to wake up and smile at me like I’m your everything, because without you, I’m not anyone’s anything.❞</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />Okay so I decided to spontaneously pick this up and I'm honestly surprised at how much I actually enjoyed this. I've been searching for a storyline similar to this and I'm glad I found it in Fighting Redemption.<br /><br />This book is far from perfect. It isn't the greatest book ever written nor is it the most original, but I still loved every single minute of it. I'm a tough romance reader because I always tend to get bored once the couple gets together but Fighting Redemption kept me interested until the very end, and that's something that rarely happens nowadays with me when it comes to romance novels.<br /><br />It does have it's flaws but they weren't bad to the point where I wanted to instantaneously put the book down. There were parts that did frustrate me especially when it came to Ryan. I felt that he was drowning in self-pity for most of the book but I can understand where he was coming from.<br /><br />In the beginning, the relationship between Fin and Ryan did feel a little insta-lovey but as the story progressed so did their relationship. I was beyond nervous every time Ryan went back out to war and my heart would feel so much for Fin when she was on her own.<br /><br />I can't really say much without giving a lot away but this was a cute, quick, little read and I'm glad I decided to pick this up! I've been looking for a modern military romance book and Fighting Redemption really fulfilled that for me.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14881697986420813615" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
