<div id="review_742494300" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/742494300" />
    <a title="Paula " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2879703-paula"><img alt="Paula " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1536687412p2/2879703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/742494300?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Paula " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Paula " href="/user/show/2879703-paula">Paula </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2879703-paula?shelf=fantabulous-favorites">fantabulous-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2879703-paula?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer742494300" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7449879929049311646"><br/><i>Fighting Redemption</i> is a deeply touching, emotionally charged, well-developed new adult romance filled with heartbreak, fiery chemistry, and loveable characters. Go ahead and grab the Kleenex, you’re going to need them. This story kept me in a constant state of tears and high emotions. I love this book hard. <br/><br/><i>
  <b>"I'll love you longer than the stars that live in the sky."</b>
</i> <br/><br/>Ryan Kendall comes from a broken home, where his father abused him and his mother ignored him. He learned at the age of seven </span>
  <span id="freeText7449879929049311646" style="display:none"><br /><i>Fighting Redemption</i> is a deeply touching, emotionally charged, well-developed new adult romance filled with heartbreak, fiery chemistry, and loveable characters. Go ahead and grab the Kleenex, you’re going to need them. This story kept me in a constant state of tears and high emotions. I love this book hard. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>"I'll love you longer than the stars that live in the sky."</b>
</i> <br /><br />Ryan Kendall comes from a broken home, where his father abused him and his mother ignored him. He learned at the age of seven about pain and suffering. His life changed for the better when he met two new students at his school. Jake, with is laidback and playful personality, immediately became Ryan’s best friend and was always by his side. Then there is Jake’s little sister, Fin, who Ryan felt an immediate attachment towards with the need to protect and, as they grew up together, silently fell in love with her. Ryan has dreamt of being a SAS solder since he was ten years old. It gives him purpose and a way to escape his broken home life.<br /><br />Finlay Tanner is a compassionate, sweet girl who loves science and has a bright future ahead of her. She eventually comes into her own as a young woman. The feelings Ryan has always had for Fin grow more every day as he watches her grow and change. He loves her, but won’t let himself have her. Not to mention he is leaving one day to join the army to start his new life. Fin has also developed feelings for Ryan. No boy can hold a candle to what she feels for Ryan. <br /><br />No words were ever spoken about their feelings towards one another, but they both knew they were there. Even if they never acted upon them. Ryan kept his distance from Fin until the time came for him and Jake (who would follow Ryan into hell) to leave for boot camp and then deployed to Afghanistan to join the war. And six years go by before Ryan and Fin see or talk again. Fin moves on with her life, eventually, during that time but never truly moves on from Ryan. She thought she had it all figured out, until Ryan finally comes back home and everything changes.<br /><br />Ryan comes back from the war older, harder, edgier, and sexier. He’s an incredible yet complicated man. He’s driven by the need to save and protect people. He’s a war hero who fights hard and loves even harder. But he’s a broken man who has never confronted the past nightmares that have shaped and molded him into the intense, tortured man he is today. If he wants to be truly happy, he must face the demons that haunt him day after day. And now that he’s back home, it’s time to face the girl that has always owned his heart. <br /><br />One of the main things that drew me to this story was the idea that two friends who grow up together eventually fall in love. Ryan goes off to war before anything develops between them, but they both continued to carry a flame for each other. The love between Fin and Ryan is one of a kind; unbreakable and deep. And, for six long years, the heart-pounding chemistry between them laid dormant… until they see each other again. The love, the passion, and the undeniable lust between them, come skyrocketing to the surface the moment they see each other again. I felt it all strongly. However, there is a lot of emotional turmoil and complicated issues between them that need to be hashed out. So much so that, as much as Fin would like to drop everything for Ryan, she can’t just let him into her heart and… into her bed. This doesn’t stop Ryan from revealing to Fin all the things he should’ve told her years ago. And the things Ryan would say to Fin… be still my heart. Ryan melted me with his honest and passionate words. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>"For six years I fought every day not to think of you, and I lost, because every day you were all I could see."-Ryan<br /><br />"Even though we've never been together, you've always been mine, and even if I never get to keep you, you'll still be mine."-Ryan</b>
</i><br /><br />As the story continues, it felt like the world was working against this couple being together. So much happens in this story with its layers upon complicated layers that revolve around unbreakable bonds, loss, grief, self-sacrifice, broken hearts, redemption, forgiveness, personal healing and, most importantly, war. Fin and Ryan had so much to overcome before they could be together. Just when you think they will finally be happy together, the story would take a turn that would make my emotions clinch – which happened often – and the tears would fall. There were scenes where my heart was pounding with every emotion expressed, every action taken, and every reason behind their words or feelings. <br /><br />This book has so much heart. I loved the beginning, the middle, and the end - which almost gave me a heart attack. I honestly felt breathless and emotionally exhausted by the last page. The scenes with Ryan in Afghanistan were depicted so realistically. I don’t know much about the military but this part of the story was well-done and intense. I would love to read more about Ryan and Jake’s army buddies and see each one of them find love. I HIGHLY recommend you grab this book ASAP! <br /><br />Rating: A<br />Heat: Warm<br /><br />-- <i>A <a href="http://romanticbookaffairs.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Romantic Book Affairs</a> Review</i><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Find us on <a href="https://twitter.com/rombookaffairs" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> and <a href="http://facebook.com/rombookaffairs" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> too!</i>
</b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7449879929049311646" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_762366377" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/762366377" />
    <a title="☆ Sammy ☆彡" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14144676-sammy"><img alt="☆ Sammy ☆彡" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1462053159p2/14144676.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/762366377?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="☆ Sammy ☆彡" class="user" itemprop="url" name="☆ Sammy ☆彡" href="/user/show/14144676-sammy">☆ Sammy ☆彡</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/19090420-fighting-redemption">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14144676-sammy?shelf=signed-books">signed-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14144676-sammy?shelf=emotionally-intense">emotionally-intense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14144676-sammy?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer762366377" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1546605976776161422"><b>What It's About</b><br/>Love * Loss * Friendship * War * Freedom * Redemption<br/><br/>Ryan Kendall knows his share of pain & loss. Growing up with an absent mother and abusive father, he dreams of joining the Australian Army in hopes of protecting and fighting for other people's freedom. He is so focused and determined to become a soldier that he sacrifices his own happiness along the way.<br/><br/><i>"being a soldier is never just about strength. It's also about knowing what you want, how hard you're willing to work for it, </i></span>
  <span id="freeText1546605976776161422" style="display:none"><b>What It's About</b><br>Love * Loss * Friendship * War * Freedom * Redemption<br><br>Ryan Kendall knows his share of pain &amp; loss. Growing up with an absent mother and abusive father, he dreams of joining the Australian Army in hopes of protecting and fighting for other people's freedom. He is so focused and determined to become a soldier that he sacrifices his own happiness along the way.<br><br><i>"being a soldier is never just about strength. It's also about knowing what you want, how hard you're willing to work for it, and what you're willing to sacrifice for it."</i><br><br>Finlay Tanner stumbled her way into Ryan's life while they were in grade school and Ryan's friendship with her older brother Jake, ensured that Ryan was always in Fin's life. For years he viewed Fin almost like a little sister, protecting her from anything he believes could cause her pain, including himself. Ryan never believed he would have anything in his life that might stand in the way of his dream of being a soldier. So at the age of nineteen, a realization of his growing feelings and attraction for Fin causes Ryan to panic and leave early for the army.<br><br>After six long years of fighting for his country and trying his best not to dwell on Fin, Ryan returns home during a break between deployments. Being around Fin again makes Ryan realize just how empty his life is without her and no matter how hard he tries he can't live his life without her. <br><br><i>"Christ. He didn't just love her, he fucking adored her. He'd give his life for her if he had to."</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396928992i/9205616.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Unfortunately, the biggest obstacle in their relationship is Ryan himself. He believes he is too broken, too damaged, and completely unworthy of a woman like Fin. He will need to find redemption and forgiveness within himself before he can move forward with his life and a relationship with Fin.<br><br><i>"This is a story about war and the cost of sacrifice. Where bonds are formed, and friendships found. Where those who are strong, fall hard. Where love is let go, heartache is born, and heroes are made. Where one man learns that the hardest fight of all, is the fight to save himself."</i><br><br><b>My Thoughts</b><br>I loved Fighting Redemption so incredibly much! I would give this beautiful story all the stars in the sky if I could &lt;333 I laughed, cried, was so completely giddy at times that I wanted to run and dance around my house, and I fell in love with Ryan Kendall! I would classify this book as one of my top reads so far in 2014 and I would list it among my favorites of all time. Please, do yourself a favor and read this book! Just make sure you have a box of tissues handy =)<br><br><i>Ebook won on Facebook giveaway from Sinfully Sexy Book reviews!</i></span>

<div id="review_721031988" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/721031988" />
    <a title="J" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10343430-j"><img alt="J" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/721031988?book_show_action=true">Sep 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="J" class="user" itemprop="url" name="J" href="/user/show/10343430-j">J</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10343430-j?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer721031988" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1337272058537642791"><b> Full Review Now Up </b> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386225699i/7315650._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>I have so much to say about this book and yet have no idea how to even put it into words. I absolutely loved every single little bit of this book. McCarthy showcases what a talented writer she truely is. <br/>The very first quote alone sets a powerful tone for the entire book:<br/><br/><br/><br/><b>There are things that we don't want to happen but have to accept, things we don't want to know but have to learn, and people we can't live without but have to let go. </b><br/><br/><br/><br/>This story begins years before the fact </span>
  <span id="freeText1337272058537642791" style="display:none"><b> Full Review Now Up </b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386225699i/7315650._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br>I have so much to say about this book and yet have no idea how to even put it into words. I absolutely loved every single little bit of this book. McCarthy showcases what a talented writer she truely is. <br>The very first quote alone sets a powerful tone for the entire book:<br><br><br><br><b>There are things that we don't want to happen but have to accept, things we don't want to know but have to learn, and people we can't live without but have to let go. </b><br><br><br><br>This story begins years before the fact when Ryan and Finlay first meet. Ryan 10 and Fin 8. <br>Being the new kids at school, Fins' brother, Jake makes quick friends with Ryan when he helps Fin up after a fall. As the years go by you watch as Ryan and Jake become Best friends. <br>With a bad home life, Ryan is always over at the Tanner's house, their home become his refuge his place to feel safe. While Ryan is aware of the connection he has with Fin, he acts indifferent to her. Quietly observing the sweet girl who deserves more than he could ever offer.<br><br>Ryan has always wanted to join the Army and as soon as he is old enough, he packs up to leave, no looking back. Fin, still in high school, watches as the boy who holds her heart walks out without giving her his own.<br><br><br><br><b>"Don't," he whispered thickly. "Please don't cry. You have such a big future ahead of you. You're going to do big things with your life. Dont let anyone stop you from being who you need to be." </b><br><br><br><br>Six years later Ryan and Jake, now SAS soldiers come home on leave. The last 6 years Ryan has had no contact with Fin. Keeping her at a distance was suppose to be the plan, but a few seconds in each others presence has everything he worked so hard on, come crashing down.<br><br>Fin has worked hard herself the last 6 years. Her career is on the fast track. She is about to make a huge career move when Ryan comes home for a visit. One look at him has her questioning where her life is meant to go. Their attraction is palpable and their pull is so strong that both are left feeling confused after each interaction. Ryan can't seem to fight his attraction to her, leaving her shocked that he even felt this way. Where is this coming from? She built a life that didn't include him and moved on. He never asked for her heart, so she did what she had to. But we see, and we feel Ryan's own internal struggle. What he lived through being away from Fin.<br><br><br><b>"I hurt too. For six years I fought every day not to think of you, and I lost, because every day you were all I could see. You were the best thing in my life- so sweet and innocent, and so goddamn tempting." </b><br><br><br><br>But their story has a long way to go. He struggles with his feelings, pushing her away. Wanting her to have a better life without him. He doesn't want to put her through the pain of what War does to people back home.<br><br><br><br><br><b>Don't hope for us, Fin. I can't have you wasting your life waiting for someone who might never return.</b><br><br><br><br>And she does, she takes her job, leaves everything behind and Ryan heads back to Duty. But when tragedy walks into her life, she must find her way through the darkness. <br><br><br><br><b>It's always the strongest that fall the hardest </b><br><br><br><br>I can't tell you what happens next without revealing too much. But this is when the story really starts to weave its heartbreaking tale. The Heartache and Pain, the Love and Tenderness, the Happiness and Laughter all of it will worm its way into your heart. And you won't want it to stop.<br>I was drowning in the pages and never wanted to surface for air. This story was beyond phenomenal<br>it moved me to tears. At times Kate's words were so poetic and insightful but also had the ability to break me down. Kate allows you to connect with Ryan, you feel his insecurities, his pain. You were there with him, hurting with him.<br><br><br><br><b>"I'm so tired," he whispered to her, his voice muffled against his knees. Hot tears fell thick and fast down his face and nothing could hold them back. He didn't even have the energy right then to hide them from her. "So tired of living with so much pain."</b><br><br><br><br>Ryan is book boyfriend perfection. It was an absolute treat to get inside his mind, and I fell even more in love with him every time we got his side. His devotion and love for Fin makes my heart smile.<br><br><br><b>"I have a thick skin baby, but you're under it. You're buried in there so deep it's like I was born with you in my soul. When I'm near you I'm consumed by you - your smile, your eyes, your heart. Even though we've never been together, you've always been mine, and even if I never get to keep you, you'll still be mine."<br><br>♥♥♥♥<br><br>"You could carry me into Hell and I'd go with you." <br>"I've been to Hell, baby," he replied. "It's the one place I'll never take you." </b><br><br><br><br><br>This book captured my heart. I wasn't sure what to expect from it but it completely blew me away. It was quite a roller-coaster of emotions. The writing was exceptional and the characters are so well written. Kate's ability to draw you in, knock you on your ass and break you down piece by piece is exactly what I crave for when I pick up a book. She left me hanging on to every scene, every page, every line. I devoured Ryan and Fin's story. Do yourself a favour and get familiar with Kate McCarthy's work, you won't be disappointed.<br><br><br><br><b>"You're all I see. Nothing holds more beauty in my eyes than you do. No one will ever love you the way I do." <br><br><br><br>☆☆☆ 5 I love you all the Stars ☆☆☆</b><br><br>Buy it <br>Read it <br>Love it</span>

<div id="review_927589436" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/927589436" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9501896-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1513212035p2/9501896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/927589436?book_show_action=true">May 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/9501896-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer927589436" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6041047126211746039">LOVED IT JUST AS MUCH THE SECOND TIME!!!<br/><br/>To say I loved this story is an understatement. This had to be one of the most beautiful books I've ever read. I'm trying to write this with tears streaming down my face. The depths of the story and the lessons it taught me will forever be engrained in my heart and soul. Beautiful. Gut wrenching. Powerful. Kate McCarthy took my breath away and I loved every word. The strength and love she created between Ryan and Fin took a hold of my heart and showed me o</span>
  <span id="freeText6041047126211746039" style="display:none">LOVED IT JUST AS MUCH THE SECOND TIME!!!<br /><br />To say I loved this story is an understatement. This had to be one of the most beautiful books I've ever read. I'm trying to write this with tears streaming down my face. The depths of the story and the lessons it taught me will forever be engrained in my heart and soul. Beautiful. Gut wrenching. Powerful. Kate McCarthy took my breath away and I loved every word. The strength and love she created between Ryan and Fin took a hold of my heart and showed me once again why I read. <br /><br />Kate took me on a journey between two of the most incredibly strong characters whose fate was written in the stars. I often say that certain books come into my life when I seem to need them. I had this one sitting on my kindle for a while now and finally had the chance to dive in. It touched my heart, squeezed it, ripped it apart and in the end, made it so incredibly full with so much love. It healed me, spoke to me, and gave me a sense of peace.<br /><br />Fighting Redemption reminded me to never take a single thing for granted, love hard and prove it with not only words, but actions. Forgive easily, laugh often, and never, ever forget to tell the people you love how much they mean to you.<br /><br />Ryan and Fin had a love that grew and grew. A type of love I can only hope my own daughters find some day. One look, one touch, one hand holding the other--I felt it through my very soul. <br /><br />"Ask me, Fin, what I see when I look up at those stars."<br />"What do you see?"<br />"You… You're all I see. Nothing holds more beauty in my eyes that you do. No one will ever love you the way I do."<br /><br />Kate, I don't know if you read these reviews, but I just want to thank you. Thank you for healing my heart just a little bit more. Thank you for making me believe that there is life beyond the sky. Thank you for reminding me to live, laugh, love and cherish every moment you're given. You are beyond incredible and I thank you for sharing your amazing gift with us. <br /><br />"…it doesn't matter if you live a billion years, or just a short handful… it's how you burn while living them that really matters.<br /><br />In Kate's words, live like you burn so bright you'll hurt someone's eyes.<br /><br />There are not enough stars in the universe for this book!!! INCREDIBLE!!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="6041047126211746039" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!

    }

      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('WaMhrsDLX9zoEFZlfJXpUHGrGyjUK2aU5Jpanq7W2mggjvkLy3i4rlsUunGMCR6X07X6qDua4DUI3bmYSSx9Aw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('pbkRjZ+8cRR9XgjCdP98nazeTTl+XRannDCvaMT668nclMkolA+WZs5a5NaEY4taDsCsuZHskAZwd0xuIwBMog==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/6876994.Kate_McCarthy">About Kate  McCarthy</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer13566554354573608681">Kate McCarthy grew up in a small town outside of Port Macquarie, Australia. Raised in a house just a short walk to the beach, Kate enjoyed the peaceful, relaxed atmosphere and friendships that come from being raised in a friendly, small town area.<br/>She now resides in Brisbane, Australia, a city in the state of Queensland where she works as an accountant, along with a sideline wedding cake business a</span>
  <span id="freeText13566554354573608681" style="display:none">Kate McCarthy grew up in a small town outside of Port Macquarie, Australia. Raised in a house just a short walk to the beach, Kate enjoyed the peaceful, relaxed atmosphere and friendships that come from being raised in a friendly, small town area.<br />She now resides in Brisbane, Australia, a city in the state of Queensland where she works as an accountant, along with a sideline wedding cake business and her writing. <br />She is married with two children, has two dogs and house in the suburbs, and a pile of friends and family dotted all over the country that help keep her sane.<br />When she’s not busy running after naughty kids, filthy dogs, crunching numbers, piping buttercream and writing books, you can find her curled up in bed in the early hours of the morning reading new books and re-reading old favourites. Her favourite books are the Black Dagger Brotherhood series by J.R. Ward in which she longs to eventually join the brotherhood and change her name to Phierce Mutha.<br />Please feel free to friend request Kate on Goodreads :D</span>
  <a data-text-id="13566554354573608681" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
